He come &amp; went all<span class='line-break'> </span> right.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Heard that Paul &amp; Earl Bennett was at<span class='line-break'> </span> Blairs.  I would of liked to see them.<span class='line-break'> </span> Heard today that Mr. Jess Adkerson [?]<span class='line-break'> </span> was dead.<span class='line-break'> </span> Talked with Fanny Emerson this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> She was at Mrs Gravelys.  Said she would<span class='line-break'> </span> come to see us be fore she went home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 clock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1588">
<h3><a name="page-1588">Monday, March 29, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The land is so wet that they<span class='line-break'> </span> cant plow.  Ben worked on a closet for Owen.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim went to Clide Reynolds with potatoes<span class='line-break'> </span> that he had solde to Clide.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got dinner.  I picked over some onions.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie &amp; the children come a while this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  Josie &amp; Carrie cut some salit for<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner tomorrow.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; Marvin went to Strait Stone this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening to see Thomson a bout the road.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben never got back until after 9 oclock.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1589">
<h3><a name="page-1589">Tuesday, March 30, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben helped rais a barn at<span class='line-break'> </span> George Blairs.  Jim worked at home.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie washed.  She has had the tooth<span class='line-break'> </span> ache all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> I staid with the baby.  This evening I<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Carries a little while.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Tonight Janie Gravely &amp; Hellen Brumfield<span class='line-break'> </span> and Franny Emerson are here to stay all <span class='line-break'> </span> night.  Orval Gravely &amp; Charley Harvey<span class='line-break'> </span> and Miss Smith &amp; Miss Carter will stay<span class='line-break'> </span> until bed time.<span class='line-break'> </span> I will be glad when they brake up.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1590">
<h3><a name="page-1590">Wednesday, March 31, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim &amp; Owen plowed this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Owen went to the mill this morning.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> ditched some today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie has had the tooth ache all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie &amp; the children come a little while<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  All they talk is good roads.<span class='line-break'> </span> Denia sent me some seed beans.  Cordie sent<span class='line-break'> </span> me some gourd seed.<span class='line-break'> </span> The children went to school.<span class='line-break'> </span> I sowed some on a quilt.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1591">
<h3><a name="page-1591">Thursday, April  1, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A rainy morning and cloudy all day.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> started to Chatham.  Got as far a Renan.<span class='line-break'> </span> Met up with Thomson and let him talk them<span class='line-break'> </span> out of going.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Jim &amp; Ben worked on the hen<span class='line-break'> </span> house.  Marvin &amp; William helped them put<span class='line-break'> </span> up the slats [?]<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie has bin suffering all day with <span class='line-break'> </span> toothache.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie come here a few minutes this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went home with her.  Come by and cut some<span class='line-break'> </span> salit.  I finished a quilt that I had been<span class='line-break'> </span> workin on.<span class='line-break'> </span> The children did not go to school.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1592">
<h3><a name="page-1592">Friday, April  2, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A rainy morning &amp; rainy again tonight.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Jim finished the hen house.<span class='line-break'> </span> I cut salit this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry went to school to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Virginia Wooding played with Edna this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Carrie this evening and got some<span class='line-break'> </span> eggs to set my hens.<span class='line-break'> </span> Tonight Effie &amp; [?]<span class='line-break'> </span> They had an entertainment<span class='line-break'> </span> at the church to night.  I would of bin glad<span class='line-break'> </span> to go but the roads is so bad that you cant<span class='line-break'> </span> run a car.<span class='line-break'> </span>  9 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1593">
<h3><a name="page-1593">Saturday, April  3, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Cloudy this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; Jim finished cleaning up the<span class='line-break'> </span> logs that come out of the olde house.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim made a cage for chickens.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> ditched.  Irvin Harvey brought his<span class='line-break'> </span> calf here to pasture.<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate come a few minutes.  Carrie come<span class='line-break'> </span> with her.  We all went to the turnip<span class='line-break'> </span> patch.  Josie carried little Mabel.<span class='line-break'> </span> The other children went to Marvins.<span class='line-break'> </span> My clock has stoped running.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1594">
<h3><a name="page-1594">Sunday, April  4, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy bad day.  Some rain.  Jim and<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and Marvin rambled a round most of the <span class='line-break'> </span> day.  A bout two oclock this morning George<span class='line-break'> </span> Blair called up Ben.  Said Hezzie [?] Andersons<span class='line-break'> </span> horse had fell in the branch.  Jim &amp; Ben went<span class='line-break'> </span> to help him.  The horse had got out.  Was not<span class='line-break'> </span> hurt much.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Johnson &amp; Reubin Reynolds passed here with a<span class='line-break'> </span> calf that had come off down this way.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie &amp; the children come a while.  Ula and<span class='line-break'> </span> Harald Mayhew come &amp; played with the children<span class='line-break'> </span> all the evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie &amp; I got dinner.  We had a chicken for<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1595">
<h3><a name="page-1595">Monday, April  5, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Rain this morning.  The branch was out of<span class='line-break'> </span> the banks.  To night it is colde and windy.<span class='line-break'> </span> We all eat dinner at home this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; Marvin Henry and Reece went to the <span class='line-break'> </span> Sulpher Springs.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie Edna Franklin and Mabel and I all went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Marvins.  Eula &amp; Harold &amp; Russel Mayhew<span class='line-break'> </span> come.  The children had some colored eggs.<span class='line-break'> </span> I think they had a good time.<span class='line-break'> </span> Johnson Reynolds was at Marvins.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim was there two.  It has bin a bad Easter.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad that we are as well as usual.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1596">
<h3><a name="page-1596">Tuesday, April  6, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A colde windy day.  Ben &amp; Jim worked on<span class='line-break'> </span> Owens spring branch.<span class='line-break'> </span> The children went to school.  Some of them<span class='line-break'> </span> had an egg hunt.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie &amp; I did what had to be done and set<span class='line-break'> </span> by the fire what we could.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben went to see Mr Jessie and John<span class='line-break'> </span> Hutcherson to day.  Did not see Mr Jessie.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> There was plenty of ice this morning.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1597">
<h3><a name="page-1597">Wednesday, April  7, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A clear colde day.  Ben &amp; Jim &amp; Owen worked on<span class='line-break'> </span> a ditch this morning.  Ben went to Strait Stone<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  The surveyor was at Thomsons.<span class='line-break'> </span> Johnson Reynolds &amp; Marvin Smith went with Ben.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie ironed.  I went to Marvins this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry &amp; Edna went to school.<span class='line-break'> </span> Lee Brumfield passed here to day.  Stoped a<span class='line-break'> </span> few minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin is here to night.  They are all at the<span class='line-break'> </span> dining room.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie is at work on Mabels flannel<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 4 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1598">
<h3><a name="page-1598">Thursday, April  8, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A clear colde windy day.  Ben went with<span class='line-break'> </span> Johnson and Mollie and Christena to Danville. <span class='line-break'> </span> Jim and Owen plowed this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie washed this morning.  I staid with<span class='line-break'> </span> Franklin &amp; Mabel.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Roy &amp; Hazel Smith come and got some flowers <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie &amp; the children come a few minutes.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Heard to night that the guano is at the<span class='line-break'> </span> Depot.  Ben has gone to Mr Mayhews to see if<span class='line-break'> </span> he wont haul for them.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Jim has gone to Marvins.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry &amp; Edna went to school.  Dr [?] come<span class='line-break'> </span> over there.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1599">
<h3><a name="page-1599">Friday, April  9, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Cloudy nearly all day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and Mr Mayhew<span class='line-break'> </span> went to the island for<span class='line-break'> </span> guano.  Mayhew hauled<span class='line-break'> </span> 4 [?] loads for the boys<span class='line-break'> </span> with his truck.  Jim plowed<span class='line-break'> </span> in his new ground this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  He plowed<span class='line-break'> </span> some in the garden and<span class='line-break'> </span> planted some things <span class='line-break'> </span> in the garden.  Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> got dinner.  She baked<span class='line-break'> </span> a cake.  Henry &amp; Edna<span class='line-break'> </span> went to school.  This<span class='line-break'> </span> evening Josie &amp; the children<span class='line-break'> </span> and I went to Marvins.<span class='line-break'> </span> I cut some turnip<span class='line-break'> </span> greens.  Henry went <span class='line-break'> </span> to Aunt Kates after<span class='line-break'> </span> some peas.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1600">
<h3><a name="page-1600">Saturday, April 10, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A clear cool day.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> plowed for Mr Mayhew.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim planted some things<span class='line-break'> </span> in the garden.  Owen<span class='line-break'> </span> plowed this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie &amp; I done one thing<span class='line-break'> </span> an other all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Marvins a<span class='line-break'> </span> few minutes this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie made Hazels<span class='line-break'> </span> hat last night.  it<span class='line-break'> </span> is very pretty I <span class='line-break'> </span> think.  Josie baked <span class='line-break'> </span> a cake and I killed <span class='line-break'> </span> a chicken for<span class='line-break'> </span> Sundays dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Owen sent us <span class='line-break'> </span> some light bread <span class='line-break'> </span> for supper.  It is very<span class='line-break'> </span> nice.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim made a hot bed to day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1601">
<h3><a name="page-1601">Sunday, April 11, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A beautiful day.  There was <span class='line-break'> </span> a big frost this morning.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> and family went to Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> Powers.  I went to George<span class='line-break'> </span> Blairs.  Ernest &amp; Lottie was<span class='line-break'> </span> there.  The girls went to <span class='line-break'> </span> Sunday School.  Otho &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> was there.  Denia had a <span class='line-break'> </span> nice dinner.  Jim eat<span class='line-break'> </span> at Carries this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr John Smith &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> his wife Owen and wife &amp; [?]was at<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvins.  Kate Harvey<span class='line-break'> </span> and Johnson Reynolds<span class='line-break'> </span> was there two.<span class='line-break'> </span> I come by.  Ben <span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Josie was at home<span class='line-break'> </span> when I got home.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got supper.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1602">
<h3><a name="page-1602">Monday, April 12, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Cloudy most of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Rain tonight.  Ben &amp; Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> planted potatoes this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Ben went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Cedar Forest for some<span class='line-break'> </span> corn that Mrs Car gave<span class='line-break'> </span> him.  Jim worked at<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  Tonight Jim went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Marvins.  Josie washed<span class='line-break'> </span> a big washing.  Kate come<span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes.  She wanted<span class='line-break'> </span> some eggs to set.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and all the kids<span class='line-break'> </span> and I went to Carries<span class='line-break'> </span> a little while.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry &amp; Edna went to <span class='line-break'> </span> school.  The surveyer<span class='line-break'> </span> was on his job today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1603">
<h3><a name="page-1603">Tuesday, April 13, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A colde windy day.  Jim <span class='line-break'> </span> and Ben &amp; Marvin went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Strait Stone this morning.  This<span class='line-break'> </span> evening Ben &amp; Marvin went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Chatham.  Jim cut<span class='line-break'> </span> wood for Kate.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie &amp; the children<span class='line-break'> </span> come down here.  Josie baked<span class='line-break'> </span> a cake for Franklins<span class='line-break'> </span> birth day.  I think the children<span class='line-break'> </span> enjoyed it.  Mollie come<span class='line-break'> </span> a little while.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry &amp; Edna went<span class='line-break'> </span> to school.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie &amp; I have not done anything in the <span class='line-break'> </span> way of settled work.<span class='line-break'> </span> Nursed [?]&amp; cooked a little.<span class='line-break'> </span> Franklin is four years<span class='line-break'> </span> olde today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:15 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1604">
<h3><a name="page-1604">Wednesday, April 14, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A clear cool day.  There<span class='line-break'> </span> was a big frost this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim &amp; Ben covered <span class='line-break'> </span> the hen house this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got dinner.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> sewed a little.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening we all<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Marvins.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry &amp; Edna<span class='line-break'> </span> went to school.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:30 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I wrote Lizzie Bennett<span class='line-break'> </span> a letter to night.<span class='line-break'> </span> I sold Nat Wooding<span class='line-break'> </span> some butter to<span class='line-break'> </span> day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1605">
<h3><a name="page-1605">Thursday, April 15, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim &amp; Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> and Owen hauled out the <span class='line-break'> </span> straw and put it on the<span class='line-break'> </span> land.  Major Rison<span class='line-break'> </span> come here to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got dinner and<span class='line-break'> </span> ironed what time <span class='line-break'> </span> she could.<span class='line-break'> </span> The school closed<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  Carrie and<span class='line-break'> </span> the children come<span class='line-break'> </span> a while this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie &amp; Carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> made Edna a hat.<span class='line-break'> </span> They embrodier it<span class='line-break'> </span> some.  I think it is <span class='line-break'> </span> pretty.  I got my<span class='line-break'> </span> check for the<span class='line-break'> </span> interest on my<span class='line-break'> </span> Liberty Bonds.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1606">
<h3><a name="page-1606">Friday, April 16, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day &amp; a little<span class='line-break'> </span> rain.  Jim &amp; Owen<span class='line-break'> </span> plowed.  Ben cleaned up<span class='line-break'> </span> the branch bank.<span class='line-break'> </span> I washed some this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  Kate Harvey<span class='line-break'> </span> come a few minutes<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I went<span class='line-break'> </span> with her as far as<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvins.  I cut some<span class='line-break'> </span> salit for dinner tomorrow.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got dinner and ironed<span class='line-break'> </span> some to night.  She<span class='line-break'> </span> looked in the range<span class='line-break'> </span> with Mabel in her<span class='line-break'> </span> arms.  Mabel put her<span class='line-break'> </span> foot out and touched<span class='line-break'> </span> the hot door and burnt<span class='line-break'> </span> her self.  I hope not <span class='line-break'> </span> bad.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1607">
<h3><a name="page-1607">Saturday, April 17, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> Owen plowed.  Ben went<span class='line-break'> </span> to see some men. This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben went to Gretna.  I<span class='line-break'> </span> went two.  Nellie &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> Evylin come with us<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  I am glad to<span class='line-break'> </span> see them.  We saw<span class='line-break'> </span> Grace and Kate as<span class='line-break'> </span> we come home.<span class='line-break'> </span> Charley Harvey<span class='line-break'> </span> is here tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben has gone to<span class='line-break'> </span> the school house<span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  Heard<span class='line-break'> </span> to day that Ren<span class='line-break'> </span> Worsham &amp; George<span class='line-break'> </span> Blair Mr Hutcherson<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Mr Anderson<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Chatham<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1608">
<h3><a name="page-1608">Sunday, April 18, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Nellie <span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Evylin has bin here<span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  The boys has bin<span class='line-break'> </span> walkin around most of <span class='line-break'> </span> the day.  Marvin and<span class='line-break'> </span> family come this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate &amp; Charley and<span class='line-break'> </span> Effie B come and<span class='line-break'> </span> staid until bed time.<span class='line-break'> </span> Effie will stay all<span class='line-break'> </span> night.  Josie and I<span class='line-break'> </span> got dinner.  Dick<span class='line-break'> </span> Wooding got his arm<span class='line-break'> </span> broke crankin his <span class='line-break'> </span> car yesterday.<span class='line-break'> </span> The patrons of the <span class='line-break'> </span> school met at<span class='line-break'> </span> the school house last <span class='line-break'> </span> night and talked a<span class='line-break'> </span> bout the school for another term.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1609">
<h3><a name="page-1609">Monday, April 19, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day. Ben and Ben plowed until noon this evening. Ben [?] &amp; Nellie and Evylin to [?] on their way home Effie Brumfield stayed with us last night. She went home as Ben went. Josie &amp; I got dinner. I went to [?] this evening. [Dr?] and Mrs Owen come while I was there to see Marvin about the road. Mabel is not well to night. Heard this evening that the guano is at the [?].<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 o clock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1610">
<h3><a name="page-1610">Tuesday, April 20, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A rainy day but not<span class='line-break'> </span> hard.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to the island<span class='line-break'> </span> after <a href='../subjects/154' title='guano'>guano</a> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some this morning.  I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Johnson Reynolds.<span class='line-break'> </span> Went by Mr Hutcherson.<span class='line-break'> </span> Talked with the snake<span class='line-break'> </span> a while.  Eat dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> at Reynolds.  Kate Harvey<span class='line-break'> </span> come down there a<span class='line-break'> </span> few minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and the children<span class='line-break'> </span> staid at home.  Mabel <span class='line-break'> </span> is sick.  Ben put <span class='line-break'> </span> on a new tire and <span class='line-break'> </span> is going to pump<span class='line-break'> </span> up his tires ready<span class='line-break'> </span> to go to Chatham.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad things <span class='line-break'> </span> is not any worse.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1611">
<h3><a name="page-1611">Wednesday, April 21, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy morning and<span class='line-break'> </span> clear this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben went to Chatham.<span class='line-break'> </span> The road question was<span class='line-break'> </span> decided to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie &amp; the children<span class='line-break'> </span> spent the day with us.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; Marvin and <span class='line-break'> </span> Jim was in Chatham.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr Owen plowed <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben brought some <span class='line-break'> </span> fish home tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> I killed a chicken<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  Mabel has<span class='line-break'> </span> bin sick all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim &amp; Ben [word omitted][?]Marvin to<span class='line-break'> </span> night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1612">
<h3><a name="page-1612">Thursday, April 22, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A beautiful day.  The men<span class='line-break'> </span> plowed all day today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel is sick.  I went<span class='line-break'> </span> off fishing.  Did not catch<span class='line-break'> </span> anything much.  I bought<span class='line-break'> </span> 7 pounds of fish.  Gave <span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie a part of them.<span class='line-break'> </span> Grace carried me.  I was <span class='line-break'> </span> glad to go but hated to<span class='line-break'> </span> leave the sick baby and<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie.  I know I will not <span class='line-break'> </span> go much more any way.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mollie was here this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening and Carrie was<span class='line-break'> </span> here a few minutes today.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am always troubled<span class='line-break'> </span> a bout some thing.  Now it<span class='line-break'> </span> is the little babe.  I do <span class='line-break'> </span> hope she will soon get <span class='line-break'> </span> well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1613">
<h3><a name="page-1613">Friday, April 23, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A clear windy day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim planted some<span class='line-break'> </span> things in the garden.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben plowed all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry cut his foot &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> and Reese steped on a nail.<span class='line-break'> </span> I hope they wont get bad <span class='line-break'> </span> off much.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel is some better<span class='line-break'> </span> off to day.  We had fish <span class='line-break'> </span> from the river for<span class='line-break'> </span> breakfast.  Josie sewed<span class='line-break'> </span> some.  I got breakfast<span class='line-break'> </span> and dinner this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim brought a little<span class='line-break'> </span> pig for us to feed<span class='line-break'> </span> up and try to <span class='line-break'> </span> make a hog.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1614">
<h3><a name="page-1614">Saturday, April 24, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Cool for this<span class='line-break'> </span> time of year.  Ben plowed with<span class='line-break'> </span> two horses.  Jim clean up<span class='line-break'> </span> the ground for him to plow.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel has cried most of<span class='line-break'> </span> the day.  I got dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> and washed dishes.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Marvins a <span class='line-break'> </span> while this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> The dogs broke up one of <span class='line-break'> </span> the hens this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna has bin crying<span class='line-break'> </span> with the tooth ache.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim &amp; Ben has<span class='line-break'> </span> gone to Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I let Nat Wooding <span class='line-break'> </span> have a pound of butter.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1615">
<h3><a name="page-1615">Sunday, April 25, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Cloudy tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> All of us stayed at home<span class='line-break'> </span> all day except Ben.<span class='line-break'> </span> He carried Mr Feris and<span class='line-break'> </span> an other man over to [?].<span class='line-break'> </span> Hugh &amp; Aubra Brumfield<span class='line-break'> </span> come and staid with Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  Marvin and family<span class='line-break'> </span> was here this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate &amp; Charley Harvey<span class='line-break'> </span> was here a little while<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and [I] got dinner.  We<span class='line-break'> </span> cooked the last sweet<span class='line-break'> </span> potatoes that we had.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1616">
<h3><a name="page-1616">Monday, April 26, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A rainy day.  The boys<span class='line-break'> </span> could not do any thing<span class='line-break'> </span> out doors.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie washed some.  Did<span class='line-break'> </span> not hang out her clothes.<span class='line-break'> </span> We had a snack for<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.  Cooked all the <span class='line-break'> </span> dried fruit and all<span class='line-break'> </span> the homony that we<span class='line-break'> </span> had.  Hazel Smith<span class='line-break'> </span> is sick.  Josies baby<span class='line-break'> </span> is better than she<span class='line-break'> </span> was last week.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got a letter from<span class='line-break'> </span> Denia Blair that<span class='line-break'> </span> gives me trouble.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am so sorrie that<span class='line-break'> </span> she is mad and dont<span class='line-break'> </span> know how to help <span class='line-break'> </span> it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1617">
<h3><a name="page-1617">Tuesday, April 27, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day &amp; rain.<span class='line-break'> </span> The men folks did not<span class='line-break'> </span> do much.  Ben worked<span class='line-break'> </span> on his car some.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; Jim &amp; Marvin &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> Owen went to Mount <span class='line-break'> </span> Airy.  Charles Harvey<span class='line-break'> </span> come down here and <span class='line-break'> </span> got the iron wedges.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie sewed some.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got dinner.  Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> went to the plant<span class='line-break'> </span> bed and got salit<span class='line-break'> </span> for dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span> We paid Irvin Lewis <span class='line-break'> </span> what we owed <span class='line-break'> </span> him today.  9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1618">
<h3><a name="page-1618">Wednesday, April 28, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A bright cool day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim got up roots [?] in the<span class='line-break'> </span> new ground.  Ben went<span class='line-break'> </span> to the island for guano<span class='line-break'> </span> late this evening.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Owen plowed.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry went to George<span class='line-break'> </span> Blairs for dahalia<span class='line-break'> </span> roots that Cordie gave<span class='line-break'> </span> me.  Floid Reynolds<span class='line-break'> </span> come for milk.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got dinner.  She<span class='line-break'> </span> put out some clothes<span class='line-break'> </span> that she washed Monday.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> as usual.  Come home<span class='line-break'> </span> and staid with the children<span class='line-break'> </span> while Josie went to<span class='line-break'> </span> the plant bed for<span class='line-break'> </span> salit.  9 oclock  </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1619">
<h3><a name="page-1619">Thursday, April 29, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Cloudy <span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  The men plowed<span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  Josie done a <span class='line-break'> </span> big washing and finished<span class='line-break'> </span> by dinner.  I got<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Johnson<span class='line-break'> </span> Reynolds.  Mollie was<span class='line-break'> </span> finishing her a silk<span class='line-break'> </span> dress.  Martha Miller<span class='line-break'> </span> was there helping<span class='line-break'> </span> her with the work<span class='line-break'> </span> a few days.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad she could<span class='line-break'> </span> get her.  We need<span class='line-break'> </span> help but cant<span class='line-break'> </span> get any.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1620">
<h3><a name="page-1620">Friday, April 30, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning.  A very<span class='line-break'> </span> windy evening.  Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Owen plowed all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben cleaned up the<span class='line-break'> </span> land.  Josie got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening she cut <span class='line-break'> </span> out a dress and <span class='line-break'> </span> made it finished ready <span class='line-break'> </span> to wear.<span class='line-break'> </span> I washed some and<span class='line-break'> </span> planted some flowers<span class='line-break'> </span> that Cordie gave<span class='line-break'> </span> me.  Mollie Reynolds<span class='line-break'> </span> come this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> and got a bucket<span class='line-break'> </span> of milk and some<span class='line-break'> </span> lillie of the valey<span class='line-break'> </span> for Reubin.  I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Carries a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes.  9:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1621">
<h3><a name="page-1621">Memorandum (iv)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>MEMORANDUM</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1622">
<h3><a name="page-1622">Saturday, May  1, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A bright cool day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim &amp; Owen worked <span class='line-break'> </span> on the land to get it<span class='line-break'> </span> ready to plant.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie ironed this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got a snack for dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> I milked and churned<span class='line-break'> </span> and fed the chickens &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> dressed a hen for dinner [?]<span class='line-break'> </span> tomorrow at dinner.  I<span class='line-break'> </span> got Ben to take me<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; the children to White <span class='line-break'> </span> Falls.  We caught a few <span class='line-break'> </span> fish.  Kate Harvey come<span class='line-break'> </span> while I was gone.  I was<span class='line-break'> </span> sorry not to see her.<span class='line-break'> </span> Charles Harvey come<span class='line-break'> </span> by this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1623">
<h3><a name="page-1623">Sunday, May  2, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben and<span class='line-break'> </span> faimily went to Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim Powers.  Mrs Car and<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr Mealer [?] was there.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim and I went to <span class='line-break'> </span> Marvins.  Carrie had<span class='line-break'> </span> a nice dinner.  Roast <span class='line-break'> </span> chicken and cocoanut<span class='line-break'> </span> pies.  Jim &amp; Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> rambled a round<span class='line-break'> </span> the plantation<span class='line-break'> </span> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1624">
<h3><a name="page-1624">Monday, May  3, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A clear cool day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; Owen planted <span class='line-break'> </span> corn.  Jim plowed in<span class='line-break'> </span> the new ground.  Josie <span class='line-break'> </span> got dinner.  She went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvins a few minutes<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I got <span class='line-break'> </span> breakfast this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> and milked the cows<span class='line-break'> </span> and fed the chickens.<span class='line-break'> </span> Worked a little in the <span class='line-break'> </span> garden then went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Kate Harveys and<span class='line-break'> </span> eat dinner then Kate<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; I went to Mags and<span class='line-break'> </span> staid a while then<span class='line-break'> </span> come home and fed <span class='line-break'> </span> the chickens then went<span class='line-break'> </span> to the plant bed for salit<span class='line-break'> </span> [?] milked.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:15 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1625">
<h3><a name="page-1625">Tuesday, May  4, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Cloudy this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Clear this evening.  The <span class='line-break'> </span> men folks plowed &amp; harrowed<span class='line-break'> </span> on their land all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie sewed a little <span class='line-break'> </span> and helped get dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> Owens.  Mrs Dews<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Mrs. Scruggs<span class='line-break'> </span> was there.<span class='line-break'> </span> We had a pleasant <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie come here<span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span> I would of bin <span class='line-break'> </span> glad if I had bin at home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 15 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1626">
<h3><a name="page-1626">Wednesday, May  5, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cool clear day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim worked on his<span class='line-break'> </span> new ground.  Ben worked<span class='line-break'> </span> on his corn land.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie washed this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  I got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening I <span class='line-break'> </span> went to Mr Edmons.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Edmons gave me<span class='line-break'> </span> 30 eggs.  I put them<span class='line-break'> </span> under hens as soon as<span class='line-break'> </span> I could after getting<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  Mrs Doss<span class='line-break'> </span> and three children<span class='line-break'> </span> come here.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben has gone to <span class='line-break'> </span> Marvins.  Dr. Owen<span class='line-break'> </span> is up there to examine<span class='line-break'> </span> them for insurance.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1627">
<h3><a name="page-1627">Thursday, May  6, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim &amp; Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Long Island<span class='line-break'> </span> for guano.  Ben &amp; Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> went a gain this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Got home a bout 10 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span> at night.  Owen plowed.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie finished Edna<span class='line-break'> </span> dress.  I got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie and her <span class='line-break'> </span> little children come<span class='line-break'> </span> a little while.  Carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> washed to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben got 100 of sugar<span class='line-break'> </span> from Thomson.  Paid<span class='line-break'> </span> 22 cts per pound.<span class='line-break'> </span> That is the highest <span class='line-break'> </span> that I ever paid for shugar.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 15 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1628">
<h3><a name="page-1628">Friday, May  7, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day and a <span class='line-break'> </span> little rain.  Jim &amp; Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> planted corn.  Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> staid at home and done<span class='line-break'> </span> the work.  She fixed me<span class='line-break'> </span> a lunch.  I gave her 25 cts.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Dews &amp; Terrow [?]<span class='line-break'> </span> went to the island.<span class='line-break'> </span> They carried me and<span class='line-break'> </span> Elsie Scruggs.  I am so<span class='line-break'> </span> glad that she let me<span class='line-break'> </span> go.  Ben carried me to<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr Dewss.  Kate <span class='line-break'> </span> come and staid a few <span class='line-break'> </span> minutes.  Am sorry but<span class='line-break'> </span> cant helpe it now.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have bin a sleep.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1629">
<h3><a name="page-1629">Saturday, May  8, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Rain this morning and<span class='line-break'> </span> a little this evening.  Clear<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  Ben carried<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim to Chatham.  Carried<span class='line-break'> </span> caned fruit and lard.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben get home before<span class='line-break'> </span> dark.  Josie ironed<span class='line-break'> </span> some and got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> I milked and churned <span class='line-break'> </span> and went to the <span class='line-break'> </span> plant bed for salit.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Carries<span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna &amp; Franklin<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Mr. Edmonds<span class='line-break'> </span> to play with Franklin<span class='line-break'> </span> Edmond.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1630">
<h3><a name="page-1630">Sunday, May  9, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A beautiful day.  Ben <span class='line-break'> </span> and family went to <span class='line-break'> </span> Rob Hubbards.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> brought back a nice<span class='line-break'> </span> mess of fish.  We cooked<span class='line-break'> </span> them tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> and eat dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie had fried<span class='line-break'> </span> chicken, the first that<span class='line-break'> </span> she had this spring.<span class='line-break'> </span> She had cherrie<span class='line-break'> </span> pies.  I did enjoy<span class='line-break'> </span> my dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1631">
<h3><a name="page-1631">Monday, May 10, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> and Mr Owen planted<span class='line-break'> </span> corn this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> This morning Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Gretna<span class='line-break'> </span> to meet Jim.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> got home about <span class='line-break'> </span> 2 oclock in the<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  Jim worked<span class='line-break'> </span> in the garden.<span class='line-break'> </span> I tried to stop <span class='line-break'> </span> the chickens out<span class='line-break'> </span> of the garden.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> We both went to <span class='line-break'> </span> Marvins this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim has gone<span class='line-break'> </span> up there tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span>  9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1632">
<h3><a name="page-1632">Tuesday, May 11, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> finished planting corn<span class='line-break'> </span> and fixed some land<span class='line-break'> </span> for water mellons seed.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim draged his new<span class='line-break'> </span> ground.  He had one<span class='line-break'> </span> of Marvins horses.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie done a big<span class='line-break'> </span> washing and sewed<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got dinner and <span class='line-break'> </span> churned this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I worked a few gourd<span class='line-break'> </span> plants and pulled dirt<span class='line-break'> </span> in the ice house hole.<span class='line-break'> </span> Went to Larries a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes then went<span class='line-break'> </span> to the plant bed<span class='line-break'> </span> for salit.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1633">
<h3><a name="page-1633">Wednesday, May 12, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day and<span class='line-break'> </span> rain tonight.  Ben and<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim and Owen fixed<span class='line-break'> </span> some of Bens tobacco land<span class='line-break'> </span> ready to plant today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got dinner and<span class='line-break'> </span> ironed some this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie come down <span class='line-break'> </span> here this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> They cut out a <span class='line-break'> </span> dress for me and got <span class='line-break'> </span> it nearly ready to wear.  I went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Johnson Reynols this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  Mrs Cook &amp; Mrs<span class='line-break'> </span> Lumpkin was there.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Cook has a cut foot.<span class='line-break'> </span> The surveyer run the<span class='line-break'> </span> line for the road today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1634">
<h3><a name="page-1634">Thursday, May 13, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day.  No rain.<span class='line-break'> </span> The boys worked on <span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco land all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> We had a shower last <span class='line-break'> </span> night.  It was badly needed.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie ironed most of <span class='line-break'> </span> the morning.  She made<span class='line-break'> </span> pies for dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> carried Josie and three<span class='line-break'> </span> children and Carrie <span class='line-break'> </span> and three children<span class='line-break'> </span> to the school house.<span class='line-break'> </span> Dr. Caton and his<span class='line-break'> </span> assistants were there<span class='line-break'> </span> to exzamine the<span class='line-break'> </span> children.  There was<span class='line-break'> </span> a crowd to be <span class='line-break'> </span> examined.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 15 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1635">
<h3><a name="page-1635">Friday, May 14, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Very cool.<span class='line-break'> </span> The men worked on the<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco land all day<span class='line-break'> </span> except Ben.  He went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Johnson Reynolds and<span class='line-break'> </span> paid for the guano <span class='line-break'> </span> and got a bushel of <span class='line-break'> </span> wheat and a bushel of<span class='line-break'> </span> cracked peas for the <span class='line-break'> </span> chickens and three<span class='line-break'> </span> bushels of peas to sow.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got dinner this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  She went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr Owens.  I washed a<span class='line-break'> </span> little this morning and<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Marvins a<span class='line-break'> </span> few minutes.  Kate Harvey<span class='line-break'> </span> was there and Charles.<span class='line-break'> </span> He carried his mother <span class='line-break'> </span> home.  9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1636">
<h3><a name="page-1636">Saturday, May 15, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A clear cool day.<span class='line-break'> </span> There was frost this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  Enough to bite<span class='line-break'> </span> tender things.  The boys<span class='line-break'> </span> finished hilling [?] up<span class='line-break'> </span> Jims new ground.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim planted some<span class='line-break'> </span> potato slips this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got dinner.  I<span class='line-break'> </span> ironed this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening I killed <span class='line-break'> </span> two chickens and<span class='line-break'> </span> churned the[n] went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Marvins.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and children<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Marvins.<span class='line-break'> </span> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1637">
<h3><a name="page-1637">Sunday, May 16, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A beautiful day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Cool for May.  There was<span class='line-break'> </span> frost this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> We all staid at home<span class='line-break'> </span> except Henry.  He went<span class='line-break'> </span> over to Renan with Reed<span class='line-break'> </span> Smith.  Marvin and Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> and Jim rambled<span class='line-break'> </span> a round most of <span class='line-break'> </span> the day.  Carrie come<span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes with<span class='line-break'> </span> the little girls.  Paul<span class='line-break'> </span> and Roy played with<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna and Franklin all<span class='line-break'> </span> the evening.  I wrote<span class='line-break'> </span> John a letter today.<span class='line-break'> </span> There has bin lots of <span class='line-break'> </span> passing here today.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span> We had our first fried chicken<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1638">
<h3><a name="page-1638">Monday, May 17, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men<span class='line-break'> </span> worked on their tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> land.  Josie staid at<span class='line-break'> </span> home and got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening she went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Marvins.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin let Reese thak [take]<span class='line-break'> </span> me fishing.  We went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Mr Jessie Worshams<span class='line-break'> </span> pond.  Did not catch <span class='line-break'> </span> any thing.  Come to<span class='line-break'> </span> the creek and fished <span class='line-break'> </span> a while.  Did not catch<span class='line-break'> </span> any thing.  I bought 10<span class='line-break'> </span> pounds of sugar from<span class='line-break'> </span> Oscar Booker.  Paid 30 cts<span class='line-break'> </span> a bushel of meal<span class='line-break'> </span> for $2.25.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1639">
<h3><a name="page-1639">Tuesday, May 18, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Cloudy but no rain<span class='line-break'> </span> to do any good.  The<span class='line-break'> </span> men folks worked on their<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco land.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie done a big washing<span class='line-break'> </span> by twelve oclock.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got dinner.  Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> kept Mabel.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie sewed some this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  Carrie and<span class='line-break'> </span> the children come <span class='line-break'> </span> a while this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and I wrote <span class='line-break'> </span> a letter and the<span class='line-break'> </span> carrier did not<span class='line-break'> </span> take them up.<span class='line-break'> </span> 8 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; Jim planted <span class='line-break'> </span> water mellon seed<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1640">
<h3><a name="page-1640">Wednesday, May 19, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A rainy morning.  We<span class='line-break'> </span> were all so glad.  Quit<span class='line-break'> </span> raining and they planted<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco.  Irvin Hardey<span class='line-break'> </span> helped them for plants.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I got breakfast &amp; milked <span class='line-break'> </span> and fed the chickens<span class='line-break'> </span> then churned and<span class='line-break'> </span> fixed up the butter.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie &amp; I got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> I cooked some<span class='line-break'> </span> onions.  The first we<span class='line-break'> </span> have cooked this <span class='line-break'> </span> year.  I drawed <span class='line-break'> </span> plants all the<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1641">
<h3><a name="page-1641">Thursday, May 20, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The boys<span class='line-break'> </span> planted some tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> today and plowed some.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and I got<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.  I churned<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Marvins.  Got some<span class='line-break'> </span> bean seed and some<span class='line-break'> </span> butter beans.  I planted<span class='line-break'> </span> the beans and gave <span class='line-break'> </span> the butter beans to<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Owen.<span class='line-break'> </span> Today is Lizzie Bennetts<span class='line-break'> </span> birth day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry &amp; Edna droped <span class='line-break'> </span> plants.  Henry pulled<span class='line-break'> </span> off my shoes tonight<span class='line-break'> </span> for me.  9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1642">
<h3><a name="page-1642">Friday, May 21, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A rainy morning.  Did<span class='line-break'> </span> not rain long.  The boys<span class='line-break'> </span> planted a little tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> then fixed land to plant.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr Owen went to George<span class='line-break'> </span> Blairs to buy corn.<span class='line-break'> </span> Did not get any.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie ironed all the<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  I cooked <span class='line-break'> </span> some onions and made <span class='line-break'> </span> a bread pudding, fried<span class='line-break'> </span> ham, and made bread<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; coffee.  Josie planted<span class='line-break'> </span> some beans this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  I did not<span class='line-break'> </span> do any thing much.<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna and I planted<span class='line-break'> </span> 180 potato slips.<span class='line-break'> </span> My lady cow has bin<span class='line-break'> </span> sick all day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1643">
<h3><a name="page-1643">Saturday, May 22, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A beautiful day.  The men<span class='line-break'> </span> fixed tobacco land all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie baked a cake this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  We cooked rice and<span class='line-break'> </span> fried meat, made coffee,<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; baked bread.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> bathed all the children,<span class='line-break'> </span> cleaned up the dining<span class='line-break'> </span> room, moved the carpet <span class='line-break'> </span> off the floor.  I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Kate Harveys and<span class='line-break'> </span> Mollie Reynolds and<span class='line-break'> </span> Carries.  I saw Lee<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield and several<span class='line-break'> </span> others.  I have gone <span class='line-break'> </span> to sleep and<span class='line-break'> </span> bot[?]ed my book.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 15 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1644">
<h3><a name="page-1644">Sunday, May 23, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim &amp; Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> staid at home until twelve.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; family went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Mr Powers this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Earl Bennett come this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening and got three<span class='line-break'> </span> pigs.  Lizzie Anderson<span class='line-break'> </span> was with him.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin &amp; Carrie and<span class='line-break'> </span> three children went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Strait Stone to preaching.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went with them. I was<span class='line-break'> </span> glad to see so many of<span class='line-break'> </span> my acquantances<span class='line-break'> </span> and enjoyed the<span class='line-break'> </span> sermond.  I come<span class='line-break'> </span> home for dinner.  We had<span class='line-break'> </span> fried chicken &amp; straw be<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie gave me a [?]<span class='line-break'> </span> of berries and cake.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1645">
<h3><a name="page-1645">Monday, May 24, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Cloudy most of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Rain this evening.  The men<span class='line-break'> </span> finished putting in guano<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  Josie staid at<span class='line-break'> </span> home all day.  Carrie and<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate come a little while<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I went <span class='line-break'> </span> to George Blairs this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  They had a quilt<span class='line-break'> </span> in.  I quilted some.<span class='line-break'> </span> They were as nice to<span class='line-break'> </span> me as they could be.<span class='line-break'> </span> They sent me home.<span class='line-break'> </span> George Jr. brought me.<span class='line-break'> </span> I saw Mr Hutcherson.<span class='line-break'> </span> He was friendly <span class='line-break'> </span> as usual.<span class='line-break'> </span> I planted some<span class='line-break'> </span> sunflower seed to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1646">
<h3><a name="page-1646">Tuesday, May 25, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A little rain this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; Jim drawed &amp; planted<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco all day.  I drawed<span class='line-break'> </span> plants this evening.  Mrs<span class='line-break'> </span> Owen helped me.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and the children<span class='line-break'> </span> Franklin &amp; Mabel <span class='line-break'> </span> went to Marvins <span class='line-break'> </span> a little while.<span class='line-break'> </span> All a bed now.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 20 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1647">
<h3><a name="page-1647">Wednesday, May 26, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day and a little<span class='line-break'> </span> rain.  The boys finished<span class='line-break'> </span> planting Bens tobacco this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  Ben went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Mount Airy this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Grace &amp; Effie Brumfield<span class='line-break'> </span> come and eat dinner <span class='line-break'> </span> with us.  They walked.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben carried them home.<span class='line-break'> </span> He bought a hay stack<span class='line-break'> </span> from Ollie Kellie.  He is<span class='line-break'> </span> to pay $40.00 for it.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie baked a cake.<span class='line-break'> </span> We killed two chickens<span class='line-break'> </span> for dinner.  Carrie &amp; the<span class='line-break'> </span> children come a little<span class='line-break'> </span> while.  Marvin got a new<span class='line-break'> </span> car to day and I am <span class='line-break'> </span> glad.  Jim planted some<span class='line-break'> </span> white beans this evening.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1648">
<h3><a name="page-1648">Thursday, May 27, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Cool and <span class='line-break'> </span> windy.  The boys planted<span class='line-break'> </span> one thing an other all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie washed a big<span class='line-break'> </span> washin.  I got a snack<span class='line-break'> </span> for dinner.  I planted<span class='line-break'> </span> some beans.  Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> planted pea nuts.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Carries.<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna and Franklin<span class='line-break'> </span> went with me.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin was replanting<span class='line-break'> </span> corn.  9 15 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1649">
<h3><a name="page-1649">Friday, May 28, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We need<span class='line-break'> </span> rain so bad.  Ben &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr Owen hauled a stack<span class='line-break'> </span> of hay from Odie Kellies.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim and Henry replanted<span class='line-break'> </span> corn.  Josie ironed and<span class='line-break'> </span> got dinner.  Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> carried Reese &amp; Edna<span class='line-break'> </span> and I to Banister <span class='line-break'> </span> River.  Ben &amp; family<span class='line-break'> </span> come after us.  We<span class='line-break'> </span> caugh a few fish.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie washed to<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  9 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1650">
<h3><a name="page-1650">Saturday, May 29, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A beautiful day.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> plowed in his corn.  Jim worked<span class='line-break'> </span> in his tobacco until twelve.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Jim &amp; Ben and<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin went to Motleys<span class='line-break'> </span> Mill to a road meeting.<span class='line-break'> </span> They got back a bout<span class='line-break'> </span> sundown.  Josie ironed<span class='line-break'> </span> all the morning<span class='line-break'> </span> and done the most of<span class='line-break'> </span> getting dinner.  This <span class='line-break'> </span> evening she bathed <span class='line-break'> </span> the children.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ada &amp; Davis Hutch<span class='line-break'> </span> erson come over<span class='line-break'> </span> here to tell me<span class='line-break'> </span> that they would<span class='line-break'> </span> take me to meeting<span class='line-break'> </span> tomorrow.  I thank them.<span class='line-break'> </span> 8 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1651">
<h3><a name="page-1651">Sunday, May 30, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The boys<span class='line-break'> </span> ramble for strawberries.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie staid at home<span class='line-break'> </span> and got dinner.  She<span class='line-break'> </span> is not feeling well.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Hutcherson kindly<span class='line-break'> </span> gave me a seat in<span class='line-break'> </span> her car and we went <span class='line-break'> </span> to old union to a <span class='line-break'> </span> meeting.  There was a<span class='line-break'> </span> big crowd and plenty<span class='line-break'> </span> to eat and sound<span class='line-break'> </span> preaching according to<span class='line-break'> </span> my way of thinking.<span class='line-break'> </span> We come by Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> Anderson Owens to<span class='line-break'> </span> see him.  He is able<span class='line-break'> </span> to sit up a little.<span class='line-break'> </span> I think he is bad <span class='line-break'> </span> off.  9 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1652">
<h3><a name="page-1652">Monday, May 31, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; Owens plowed corn.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and got dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> and churned.<span class='line-break'> </span> After dinner Edna<span class='line-break'> </span> and I went to try<span class='line-break'> </span> and get some straw<span class='line-break'> </span> berries.  We got a few.<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate Harvey come<span class='line-break'> </span> while I was gone.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin &amp; Carrie <span class='line-break'> </span> and the girls went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Altavista.  Paul<span class='line-break'> </span> and Roy staid here.<span class='line-break'> </span> Reese plowed.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1653">
<h3><a name="page-1653">Memorandum (v)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>May the first 1920<span class='line-break'> </span> I gave Ben $2:00<span class='line-break'> </span> to take me to<span class='line-break'> </span> White Falls</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1654">
<h3><a name="page-1654">Tuesday, June  1, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We need<span class='line-break'> </span> rain very bad.  The men<span class='line-break'> </span> folks finished plowing<span class='line-break'> </span> over their corn this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  Ben &amp; Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> and Franklin and<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Long<span class='line-break'> </span> Island.  I fished a<span class='line-break'> </span> little while.  Caught<span class='line-break'> </span> a little cat fish.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben bought a few<span class='line-break'> </span> things from [?]<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie done a big washing<span class='line-break'> </span> to day and ironed<span class='line-break'> </span> some this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie &amp; the children<span class='line-break'> </span> come a little whil<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I am a<span class='line-break'> </span> sleep and blot my<span class='line-break'> </span> book.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 15 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span> Note written upside down across<span class='line-break'> </span> the top of the page: I got a box<span class='line-break'> </span> of shells that John sent me.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1655">
<h3><a name="page-1655">Wednesday, June  2, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben &amp; Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> worked in the tobaco<span class='line-break'> </span> some.  Josie ironed<span class='line-break'> </span> and got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> I washed a little.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin Smith<span class='line-break'> </span> went to the mill.<span class='line-break'> </span> Reese &amp; Paul and <span class='line-break'> </span> I went with <span class='line-break'> </span> him.  We went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Cedar Forest.<span class='line-break'> </span> [?] Anderson<span class='line-break'> </span> ground his grain.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1656">
<h3><a name="page-1656">Thursday, June  3, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Some clouds<span class='line-break'> </span> but no rain here.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim &amp; Ben worked on<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco until dinner then<span class='line-break'> </span> they &amp; Josie and three<span class='line-break'> </span> of the children went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Mr Bill Tuckers<span class='line-break'> </span> burial and then to<span class='line-break'> </span> Chatham.  I do hope<span class='line-break'> </span> they got there ok.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got supper.<span class='line-break'> </span> Reese &amp; Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> and I eat.  I milked.<span class='line-break'> </span> The boys fed the<span class='line-break'> </span> horses &amp; hogs.<span class='line-break'> </span> Now we are ready<span class='line-break'> </span> to go to bed.<span class='line-break'> </span> Reese and Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> will sleep in my<span class='line-break'> </span> room.<span class='line-break'> </span> 8 30 </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1657">
<h3><a name="page-1657">Friday, June  4, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy all day and<span class='line-break'> </span> a little rain.  Enough<span class='line-break'> </span> to do lots of good.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim &amp; Ben Josie and<span class='line-break'> </span> the children come<span class='line-break'> </span> home to day at<span class='line-break'> </span> twelve.  They had<span class='line-break'> </span> a good time but<span class='line-break'> </span> huriedly they had<span class='line-break'> </span> the babys pictures<span class='line-break'> </span> made.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Johnson<span class='line-break'> </span> Reynolds this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mollie &amp; Christenia<span class='line-break'> </span> was going to Lee Brumfields.<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate Harvey come<span class='line-break'> </span> after potato slips.<span class='line-break'> </span> Robert brought<span class='line-break'> </span> me home.  Ben had<span class='line-break'> </span> started after me.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1658">
<h3><a name="page-1658">Saturday, June  5, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A rainy morning and<span class='line-break'> </span> that was what we needed.<span class='line-break'> </span> The boys planted some<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco.  Kate &amp; Irvin<span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey come after plants.<span class='line-break'> </span> They were here for dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> They got a few plants <span class='line-break'> </span> and went home.<span class='line-break'> </span> We had cabbage for dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben carried my heifer<span class='line-break'> </span> to Reynolds.  Ben &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> Jim brought Bell<span class='line-break'> </span> home from Mr Laynes.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie made Ben a <span class='line-break'> </span> shirt to day.  I ironed<span class='line-break'> </span> some.  I thined my<span class='line-break'> </span> beets and parsnips<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9:15 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span> The bees swarmed to day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1659">
<h3><a name="page-1659">Sunday, June  6, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A beautiful day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Cool for June.  We all<span class='line-break'> </span> was at home for dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> We had peas and chicken<span class='line-break'> </span> and chocolate pies.<span class='line-break'> </span> All of us went <span class='line-break'> </span> to Marvins this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  We went<span class='line-break'> </span> to see the new road.  Richard<span class='line-break'> </span> Wooding &amp; family <span class='line-break'> </span> passed on his <span class='line-break'> </span> car.  He ask some<span class='line-break'> </span> of us to ride.  Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> and the baby and<span class='line-break'> </span> Franklin rode home.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was so glad that she<span class='line-break'> </span> could ride as she<span class='line-break'> </span> had to carrie the<span class='line-break'> </span> baby.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 15 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1660">
<h3><a name="page-1660">Monday, June  7, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr Owen finished plant<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco.  Ben replanting<span class='line-break'> </span> his.  Marvin and his<span class='line-break'> </span> crowd went to Kates<span class='line-break'> </span> and helped Irvin<span class='line-break'> </span> finish planting his crop.<span class='line-break'> </span> I drawed a few<span class='line-break'> </span> plants.  Josie got<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner and made<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben a shirt.  We<span class='line-break'> </span> cooked turnip salit<span class='line-break'> </span> for dinner and had<span class='line-break'> </span> corn bread.  I did<span class='line-break'> </span> enjoy it.  I got an <span class='line-break'> </span> invatation to the school<span class='line-break'> </span> at Charlottsvill.  Bruce<span class='line-break'> </span> Reynolds sent it.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1661">
<h3><a name="page-1661">Tuesday, June  8, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben worked<span class='line-break'> </span> on the land for peas.<span class='line-break'> </span> Owen plowed corn.  Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> made a crate for the<span class='line-break'> </span> calf and worked<span class='line-break'> </span> some in the garden<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> plowed some.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie done a big<span class='line-break'> </span> washing.  Got done by<span class='line-break'> </span> twelve.  I got <span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin let Reese<span class='line-break'> </span> take me to White<span class='line-break'> </span> Falls.  He made the <span class='line-break'> </span> trip ok.  I am so<span class='line-break'> </span> glad that nothing happened.<span class='line-break'> </span> Virginia Wooding spent<span class='line-break'> </span> the day with Edna.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 30 ocl<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1662">
<h3><a name="page-1662">Wednesday, June  9, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim and<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin &amp; Reese went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Gretna and carried<span class='line-break'> </span> the calves.  Ben &amp; Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> plowed and sowed<span class='line-break'> </span> peas.  Mr Owen plowed<span class='line-break'> </span> in his corn.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie and the children<span class='line-break'> </span> come down here.<span class='line-break'> </span> Janie &amp; Aubra<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield come this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.
