I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Johnson Reynolds.<span class='line-break'> </span> Johnson come and<span class='line-break'> </span> got a cat and 3<span class='line-break'> </span> kittens.  We got a <span class='line-break'> </span> barrel of flour to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1663">
<h3><a name="page-1663">Thursday, June 10, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben and<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim and Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> worked tobacco most of<span class='line-break'> </span> the day.  Josie and <span class='line-break'> </span> I got dinner.  We made<span class='line-break'> </span> some preserves of dew<span class='line-break'> </span> beries that was caned<span class='line-break'> </span> also some peaches.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie sewed some<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> went to Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> a little while.<span class='line-break'> </span> Miss Bell and Miss<span class='line-break'> </span> Christenia Wooding<span class='line-break'> </span> was there.  I was<span class='line-break'> </span> glad to see them.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin was working<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1664">
<h3><a name="page-1664">Friday, June 11, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We had a<span class='line-break'> </span> little shower.  Jim &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben worked tobacco and<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry Edna went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Johnson Reynolds for<span class='line-break'> </span> a few butter beans.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> I washed a little.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and the children<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Marvins a<span class='line-break'> </span> few minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to the <span class='line-break'> </span> plant beds for<span class='line-break'> </span> salit.<span class='line-break'> </span> Tom Edmons come <span class='line-break'> </span> for some vinegar.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span> Virginia Harvey come<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning for some <span class='line-break'> </span> butter.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1665">
<h3><a name="page-1665">Saturday, June 12, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim &amp; Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> and Henry worked<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco and planted potato<span class='line-break'> </span> slips.  Ben has gone to<span class='line-break'> </span> Strait Stone tonight<span class='line-break'> </span> to the Lodge.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie ironed all the <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  Bathed and<span class='line-break'> </span> dressed the children.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got breakfast and<span class='line-break'> </span> milked the cows fed<span class='line-break'> </span> the chickens then I <span class='line-break'> </span> went to Mr Mayhews<span class='line-break'> </span> and Mr Edmons s<span class='line-break'> </span> for potatoe slips.<span class='line-break'> </span> Got a few at both places.<span class='line-break'> </span> Beatrice and Dewie<span class='line-break'> </span> come down here this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> They said that the baby<span class='line-break'> </span> was sick.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1666">
<h3><a name="page-1666">Sunday, June 13, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at home all day.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Mount Airy<span class='line-break'> </span> to get ice.  Did not get<span class='line-break'> </span> any.  Come by Renan &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> brought Kate Harvey<span class='line-break'> </span> home with him.  He had<span class='line-break'> </span> all the children with<span class='line-break'> </span> him.  He then went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Strait Stone and got ice.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie made cream<span class='line-break'> </span> for dinner.  We had<span class='line-break'> </span> our first snaps and<span class='line-break'> </span> beets.  We had fried<span class='line-break'> </span> chicken.  Marvin and<span class='line-break'> </span> family was here a<span class='line-break'> </span> few minutes this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Reese Smith carried Aunt<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate home.  Henry too.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1667">
<h3><a name="page-1667">Monday, June 14, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men<span class='line-break'> </span> folks worked tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and I got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> We had ice cream.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie has bin sick <span class='line-break'> </span> most of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Nothing much happened <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 : oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1668">
<h3><a name="page-1668">Tuesday, June 15, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  There was<span class='line-break'> </span> a little rain this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> and this evening but not<span class='line-break'> </span> enough to do any good.<span class='line-break'> </span> The men folks worked<span class='line-break'> </span> on their tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> She had snaps and<span class='line-break'> </span> potatoes.  I planted <span class='line-break'> </span> some butter beans<span class='line-break'> </span> and thined some<span class='line-break'> </span> corn.  Josie and<span class='line-break'> </span> the children<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Marvins <span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span> While she was <span class='line-break'> </span> gone two of the <span class='line-break'> </span> Doss children<span class='line-break'> </span> came and wanted <span class='line-break'> </span> to see Josie a bout<span class='line-break'> </span> cutting out some sewing.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1669">
<h3><a name="page-1669">Wednesday, June 16, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A clear hot day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim worked in his<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco.  Ben went<span class='line-break'> </span> to the mill mighily<span class='line-break'> </span> a gainst his will.<span class='line-break'> </span> He let Henry and<span class='line-break'> </span> I go with him.  We<span class='line-break'> </span> fished. Caught 14.  Had<span class='line-break'> </span> them for dinner.  Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> got dinner.  She had <span class='line-break'> </span> chicken.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span> One of the cows is<span class='line-break'> </span> sick.  I do hope she<span class='line-break'> </span> will get well.<span class='line-break'> </span> Eva Smith is not<span class='line-break'> </span> well.  I hope she may<span class='line-break'> </span> get well soon.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1670">
<h3><a name="page-1670">Thursday, June 17, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We need<span class='line-break'> </span> rain so bad.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim staid a bout<span class='line-break'> </span> home and worked tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> some.  Ben carried<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and all the<span class='line-break'> </span> children except Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> to Jim Powers.  I got<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner and churned.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went with Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> to Powers this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Car was not<span class='line-break'> </span> there.  Max was there.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Epperson/Efferson[?] and<span class='line-break'> </span> several of her<span class='line-break'> </span> children was there.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1671">
<h3><a name="page-1671">Friday, June 18, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim and<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben thined corn until<span class='line-break'> </span> twelve oclock.  Jim <span class='line-break'> </span> went to Chatham<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> carried him to<span class='line-break'> </span> Gretna.  I went<span class='line-break'> </span> with them.  Lees<span class='line-break'> </span> folks was workin<span class='line-break'> </span> in their tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span> Grace gave me some<span class='line-break'> </span> cabbage.  I am glad<span class='line-break'> </span> of them.  Josie washed.<span class='line-break'> </span> We come by Kates<span class='line-break'> </span> from Gretna.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Owen was there<span class='line-break'> </span> and Christenia Reynolds.<span class='line-break'> </span> Charles and a <span class='line-break'> </span> work man was at work<span class='line-break'> </span> on the house.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1672">
<h3><a name="page-1672">Saturday, June 19, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Rain the most of the<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  Ben replanted<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco and Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> replanted all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie made Edna <span class='line-break'> </span> a dress.  I got most<span class='line-break'> </span> of the dinner.  We <span class='line-break'> </span> had cabbage.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> enjoyed them.<span class='line-break'> </span> I planted a few <span class='line-break'> </span> butter beans then<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Marvins.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie was have<span class='line-break'> </span> a time keeping<span class='line-break'> </span> the boys in from <span class='line-break'> </span> the rain.<span class='line-break'> </span> 8 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Short is at<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr Owens tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1673">
<h3><a name="page-1673">Sunday, June 20, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A rainy day.  Just<span class='line-break'> </span> what we needed.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim come from Chatham<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  Bruce<span class='line-break'> </span> Reynolds brought<span class='line-break'> </span> him.  We all have <span class='line-break'> </span> staid at home all<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  Josie and I got<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.  We fried<span class='line-break'> </span> chicken and had<span class='line-break'> </span> peas and potatoes <span class='line-break'> </span> and corn starch <span class='line-break'> </span> pudding.  There has<span class='line-break'> </span> bin very little<span class='line-break'> </span> passin here today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr Mayhew<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; some of his family<span class='line-break'> </span> on thier truck is all<span class='line-break'> </span> that passed that I saw.<span class='line-break'> </span> 8 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1674">
<h3><a name="page-1674">Monday, June 21, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day most of <span class='line-break'> </span> the day.  Had a shower<span class='line-break'> </span> late this evening.  Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> and three children <span class='line-break'> </span> went to Kate Harveys<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Had started<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  The rain came so <span class='line-break'> </span> quick that they went in<span class='line-break'> </span> the barn at Reynolds.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben went to meet them.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben cut some wheat<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> twice to day.  Did <span class='line-break'> </span> not stay much<span class='line-break'> </span> either time.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1675">
<h3><a name="page-1675">Tuesday, June 22, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men<span class='line-break'> </span> thined corn and then<span class='line-break'> </span> cut wheat.<span class='line-break'> </span> Franklin has bin very<span class='line-break'> </span> sick all day.  I do hope<span class='line-break'> </span> he will be better<span class='line-break'> </span> by morning.  Two of <span class='line-break'> </span> the Hubbard girls <span class='line-break'> </span> washed for Josie <span class='line-break'> </span> today.  I got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Reese carried me<span class='line-break'> </span> to White Falls.  The<span class='line-break'> </span> river was so<span class='line-break'> </span> muddy that we<span class='line-break'> </span> could no fish and<span class='line-break'> </span> catch any thing.<span class='line-break'> </span> We come by Mount<span class='line-break'> </span> Airy and bough<span class='line-break'> </span> a few things.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1676">
<h3><a name="page-1676">Wednesday, June 23, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A rainy morning.   Clear<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  Jim &amp; Ben plowed<span class='line-break'> </span> some in the corn until the<span class='line-break'> </span> land got two wet.<span class='line-break'> </span> They cut wheat this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening, finished Owens<span class='line-break'> </span> and cut some on Jims.<span class='line-break'> </span> Charles &amp; Jack Harvey<span class='line-break'> </span> come down here a little<span class='line-break'> </span> while this evening.  Jack<span class='line-break'> </span> was going to Richmon<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  At least start<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  Franklin is sick<span class='line-break'> </span> but we hope he will<span class='line-break'> </span> getting better.  I got <span class='line-break'> </span> dinner and ironed<span class='line-break'> </span> some.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1677">
<h3><a name="page-1677">Thursday, June 24, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Clouds a<span class='line-break'> </span> round but very little rain.<span class='line-break'> </span> We hope Franklin is improve.<span class='line-break'> </span> They had the Dr to see him <span class='line-break'> </span> last night.  Ben and Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> plowed corn a while<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning then cut<span class='line-break'> </span> Jims wheat &amp; finished<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvins wheat.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got most of the<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.  We had snaps<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; potatoes and beets<span class='line-break'> </span> and fried chicken.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim plowed some in<span class='line-break'> </span> the garden this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> The garden is lookin<span class='line-break'> </span> well now.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1678">
<h3><a name="page-1678">Friday, June 25, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The boys<span class='line-break'> </span> plowed in the corn<span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  Josie and I got<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.  Franklin is<span class='line-break'> </span> improving we think.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to see Mollie<span class='line-break'> </span> Reynolds this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mollie &amp; Betty Haley<span class='line-break'> </span> was ironing.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie baked a cake<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Josie ironed<span class='line-break'> </span> and baked a cake<span class='line-break'> </span> and was feeling<span class='line-break'> </span> badly when I got<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  Heard today<span class='line-break'> </span> that Howard Fontine<span class='line-break'> </span> was married.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1679">
<h3><a name="page-1679">Saturday, June 26, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben and<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim finished plowing their<span class='line-break'> </span> corn for this year.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> plowed tobacco the [?]<span class='line-break'> </span> of the day.  Josie washed<span class='line-break'> </span> a little and ironed<span class='line-break'> </span> some and baked a <span class='line-break'> </span> cake and bathed <span class='line-break'> </span> the children.  I got <span class='line-break'> </span> breakfast and milked<span class='line-break'> </span> the cows.  Brough the milk<span class='line-break'> </span> from the spring and churned,<span class='line-break'> </span> gathered some snaps, got <span class='line-break'> </span> some potatoes and [?]<span class='line-break'> </span> them and cooked them, dress<span class='line-break'> </span> 4 chickens.  Went to <span class='line-break'> </span> Marvins and helped Carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> dress 4 chickens.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> are fixin for a dinner at<span class='line-break'> </span> Strait Stone tomorrow.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span> [Written upside down above the<span class='line-break'> </span> date: We hope that Franklin is <span class='line-break'> </span> getting on ok.  Henry is complaining<span class='line-break'> </span> to night.]</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1680">
<h3><a name="page-1680">Sunday, June 27, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We got<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner for the meeting.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went with Ben.<span class='line-break'> </span> They had a big<span class='line-break'> </span> crowd and plenty <span class='line-break'> </span> to eat.  I come<span class='line-break'> </span> home with Lizzie<span class='line-break'> </span> and went to <span class='line-break'> </span> [?] to Sunday<span class='line-break'> </span> School entertaining.<span class='line-break'> </span> Am at Lizzies<span class='line-break'> </span> to night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1681">
<h3><a name="page-1681">Monday, June 28, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Lizzie<span class='line-break'> </span> and I walked to see<span class='line-break'> </span> Ola Jefferson.  Lonny<span class='line-break'> </span> Bennett come after us.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mary Fowler &amp; Annie<span class='line-break'> </span> [?] had come to<span class='line-break'> </span> see me.  I was so<span class='line-break'> </span> glad that they come.<span class='line-break'> </span> Alma carried<span class='line-break'> </span> them home and got<span class='line-break'> </span> ice.  They had ice<span class='line-break'> </span> cream at supper.<span class='line-break'> </span> Tom B. and [?] I<span class='line-break'> </span> and Paul B and Ed<span class='line-break'> </span> Mayhew went to see<span class='line-break'> </span> some land solde near<span class='line-break'> </span> Brook neal.  Theye did<span class='line-break'> </span> not buy any land.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1682">
<h3><a name="page-1682">Tuesday, June 29, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  I am at<span class='line-break'> </span> Jims yet.  Ola Jefferson<span class='line-break'> </span> spent the day here.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Alma<span class='line-break'> </span> and Ola went to [?]<span class='line-break'> </span> Lizzie kept the children.<span class='line-break'> </span> Tonight Lonnie <span class='line-break'> </span> carried [?] &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> Lizzie and I to<span class='line-break'> </span> Billie Bennetts.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to go.<span class='line-break'> </span> I would like<span class='line-break'> </span> to know what <span class='line-break'> </span> they are doing at<span class='line-break'> </span> home.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1683">
<h3><a name="page-1683">Wednesday, June 30, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day at<span class='line-break'> </span> Tims yet.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Lizzie<span class='line-break'> </span> and I went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Gordon Bennetts<span class='line-break'> </span> to see Frances<span class='line-break'> </span> Bennett &amp; her mother.<span class='line-break'> </span> They were getting<span class='line-break'> </span> on fine.<span class='line-break'> </span> Tonight Alma &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> Paul and Lonnie <span class='line-break'> </span> has gone to Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> Mayhews.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I would be so <span class='line-break'> </span> glad to know how<span class='line-break'> </span> they are getting on<span class='line-break'> </span> at home.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1684">
<h3><a name="page-1684">Thursday, July  1, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Very warm.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have bin here at<span class='line-break'> </span> Tim Bennetts all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Tim and Gorden went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Chatham.<span class='line-break'> </span> Tim said that Lee<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield was there.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Jefferson and<span class='line-break'> </span> Miss Estell Riddle<span class='line-break'> </span> to Tims.<span class='line-break'> </span> Well I don't know<span class='line-break'> </span> to write.<span class='line-break'> </span> Wish I could hear<span class='line-break'> </span> from home.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1685">
<h3><a name="page-1685">Friday, July  2, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  I come<span class='line-break'> </span> home this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> from Tim Bennetts.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin brought me<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  We come by<span class='line-break'> </span> the Ward olde place.<span class='line-break'> </span> The land there was sold<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  I found all<span class='line-break'> </span> well.  Charley &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> Irvin Harvey and<span class='line-break'> </span> Miss Fanny Power <span class='line-break'> </span> and Miss Bettie Moses<span class='line-break'> </span> and Effie Brumfield<span class='line-break'> </span> and Virginia Harvey<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Banister<span class='line-break'> </span> Bridge and went in<span class='line-break'> </span> batheing.  Got back<span class='line-break'> </span> here at 9 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span> and eat supper.<span class='line-break'> </span> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1686">
<h3><a name="page-1686">Saturday, July  3, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Fanny &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> Effie Power &amp; Brumfield<span class='line-break'> </span> was here to day.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> carried them to Lee<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfields this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben finished cutting<span class='line-break'> </span> oats this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening he went <span class='line-break'> </span> to Cedar Forest.<span class='line-break'> </span> He carried Josie and<span class='line-break'> </span> all the children<span class='line-break'> </span> and I.  I went<span class='line-break'> </span> with them to the creek.<span class='line-break'> </span> While they bathed I <span class='line-break'> </span> fished.  Caught 7 fish.<span class='line-break'> </span> We got home on time<span class='line-break'> </span> to do our work.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie has bin <span class='line-break'> </span> sick to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> It is raining.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1687">
<h3><a name="page-1687">Sunday, July  4, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day but windy.<span class='line-break'> </span> We all staid at home <span class='line-break'> </span> until after dinner except<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna.  She went to Sunday<span class='line-break'> </span> School with Marvin.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went with Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> and Carrie to Gretna<span class='line-break'> </span> to meet Jim.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr Emet and Dr Will<span class='line-break'> </span> Smith and their wives <span class='line-break'> </span> come to Marvins a<span class='line-break'> </span> few minutes this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  Doris &amp; Janie<span class='line-break'> </span> and Christenia Rey<span class='line-break'> </span> nolds come and<span class='line-break'> </span> staid a while this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1688">
<h3><a name="page-1688">Monday, July  5, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben plowed in the <span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Ben went<span class='line-break'> </span> with the machine.<span class='line-break'> </span> They thrashed wheat<span class='line-break'> </span> at Ren Worshams<span class='line-break'> </span> and Willie Mayhews.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Carries.  Kate<span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey was there.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry wormed<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> He is sick tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben eat supper<span class='line-break'> </span> at Willies Mayhews<span class='line-break'> </span> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span> There was a big<span class='line-break'> </span> time in Altavista<span class='line-break'> </span> today.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1689">
<h3><a name="page-1689">Tuesday, July  6, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben &amp; Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> went and helped<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr Edmons and Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> Layne thrash wheat<span class='line-break'> </span> then they thrashed<span class='line-break'> </span> here and at Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> and Reynols.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and I got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Several of the men<span class='line-break'> </span> eat with us.<span class='line-break'> </span> Maybel was sick<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  Carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> come a few minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to look<span class='line-break'> </span> for Berries.  Could <span class='line-break'> </span> not find any to<span class='line-break'> </span> do any good.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1690">
<h3><a name="page-1690">Wednesday, July  7, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning and a <span class='line-break'> </span> good rain this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim plowed some<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  Ben was with<span class='line-break'> </span> the machine.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie washed two<span class='line-break'> </span> Preachers [?] come here<span class='line-break'> </span> a little while today.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna hurt Maybels<span class='line-break'> </span> finger with the <span class='line-break'> </span> bell.  I am so sorry.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got a litter<span class='line-break'> </span> from Effie Brumfield<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> 8:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1691">
<h3><a name="page-1691">Thursday, July  8, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Very warm.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; Jim finished<span class='line-break'> </span> laying by Bens<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> and ironed some<span class='line-break'> </span> then went to Marvins.<span class='line-break'> </span> Reese &amp; Henry and <span class='line-break'> </span> I went to White<span class='line-break'> </span> Falls.  I caught a <span class='line-break'> </span> few fish.  The <span class='line-break'> </span> river was mudy.<span class='line-break'> </span> I brought home<span class='line-break'> </span> a bushel of meal.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie and I togather<span class='line-break'> </span> sold 8 doz eggs<span class='line-break'> </span> at 35 cts per doz.<span class='line-break'> </span> All of us are reason<span class='line-break'> </span> able well.  I hope I am<span class='line-break'> </span> thanksful.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1692">
<h3><a name="page-1692">Friday, July  9, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben has<span class='line-break'> </span> bin with the machine<span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  Jim plowed<span class='line-break'> </span> some.  Mr Owen and<span class='line-break'> </span> Board Dews plowed <span class='line-break'> </span> in Owens tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie ironed nearly <span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  I got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie come a while<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to George<span class='line-break'> </span> Blairs.  Found<span class='line-break'> </span> them all well.<span class='line-break'> </span> Rens little girls was there learning<span class='line-break'> </span> to crosha.<span class='line-break'> </span> I stoped at Hutchersons<span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1693">
<h3><a name="page-1693">Saturday, July 10, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; Jim helped<span class='line-break'> </span> thrash wheat at George<span class='line-break'> </span> Blairs today.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> went for Mrs Car<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> has bin sick all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Dr Owen was in <span class='line-break'> </span> to see her this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  I do hope<span class='line-break'> </span> she may be well<span class='line-break'> </span> soon.  I scrubed<span class='line-break'> </span> the things in the cook<span class='line-break'> </span> room this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim went to Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Was<span class='line-break'> </span> there when it<span class='line-break'> </span> commenced raining.<span class='line-break'> </span> We have had a good<span class='line-break'> </span> rain and it is raining<span class='line-break'> </span> now.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1694">
<h3><a name="page-1694">Sunday, July 11, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Cloudy and some rain.<span class='line-break'> </span> We all have bin at<span class='line-break'> </span> home all day.  We had a<span class='line-break'> </span> surprise.  Billie and Nanie<span class='line-break'> </span> Bennett and Allen and <span class='line-break'> </span> Elsie Boling come.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad that they<span class='line-break'> </span> come.  Hope that they<span class='line-break'> </span> got home O K.  Would<span class='line-break'> </span> like to know.<span class='line-break'> </span> I would of liked to<span class='line-break'> </span> had things better but<span class='line-break'> </span> am glad things were <span class='line-break'> </span> no worse.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie baked some<span class='line-break'> </span> pies for me.  I was<span class='line-break'> </span> very glad of them.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1695">
<h3><a name="page-1695">Monday, July 12, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  A little<span class='line-break'> </span> rain.  Jim mowed some<span class='line-break'> </span> grass.  Ben topped<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> They helped thrash<span class='line-break'> </span> wheat for Mr Dews.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got dinner this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  I went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvins.  Kate Harvey<span class='line-break'> </span> come there and<span class='line-break'> </span> come with me home.<span class='line-break'> </span> Charles Harvey was<span class='line-break'> </span> here and carried <span class='line-break'> </span> his mother home.<span class='line-break'> </span> At this time the crop<span class='line-break'> </span> is lookin well.<span class='line-break'> </span> As good as I ever<span class='line-break'> </span> saw on this place.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1696">
<h3><a name="page-1696">Tuesday, July 13, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben went<span class='line-break'> </span> to thrash wheat.  Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> hauled up the oats <span class='line-break'> </span> and hay.  Josie and<span class='line-break'> </span> I got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Nellie &amp; Evylin come<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Denia Blair come<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I was<span class='line-break'> </span> glad.<span class='line-break'> </span> Hutchersons quit<span class='line-break'> </span> thrashing to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was<span class='line-break'> </span> I have not seen <span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1697">
<h3><a name="page-1697">Wednesday, July 14, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> carried Mrs Car home<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  Henry &amp; I<span class='line-break'> </span> went with him.  Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> wormed tobacco this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Picked black berries<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Reese carried me to<span class='line-break'> </span> White Falls this eve.<span class='line-break'> </span> I caught a few fish.<span class='line-break'> </span> The river was muddy.<span class='line-break'> </span> I helped Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> get dinner.  Harvey<span class='line-break'> </span> Charles &amp; Virginia<span class='line-break'> </span> is here to night.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mollie Reynolds was<span class='line-break'> </span> at Marvins.  A lot of<span class='line-break'> </span> girls went to<span class='line-break'> </span> the pond this eve.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1698">
<h3><a name="page-1698">Thursday, July 15, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim <span class='line-break'> </span> and Ben jobed<span class='line-break'> </span> a round until twelve<span class='line-break'> </span> then Ben went to <span class='line-break'> </span> Mr Dews and worked<span class='line-break'> </span> on his car until<span class='line-break'> </span> night.  Nellie Brumfield<span class='line-break'> </span> made some preserves.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and I was<span class='line-break'> </span> washing.  Bettie<span class='line-break'> </span> Haley came and<span class='line-break'> </span> finished for us.<span class='line-break'> </span> Evylin Brumfield<span class='line-break'> </span> is sick.  Jim and <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben has gone to<span class='line-break'> </span> Dr Owens to night.<span class='line-break'> </span> I do hope she <span class='line-break'> </span> may soon be <span class='line-break'> </span> better.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1699">
<h3><a name="page-1699">Friday, July 16, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> and Ben worked on<span class='line-break'> </span> the barn shelter.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; Josie went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Jim Thomsons<span class='line-break'> </span> and got pears to<span class='line-break'> </span> preserve.  Nellie<span class='line-break'> </span> got some berries<span class='line-break'> </span> to make jellie.<span class='line-break'> </span> I made 16 glasses<span class='line-break'> </span> of jellie this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> and made three <span class='line-break'> </span> quarts of jam.<span class='line-break'> </span> Evylin has not<span class='line-break'> </span> come down stairs<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  Hope she<span class='line-break'> </span> will be a bout<span class='line-break'> </span> in the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got some snaps<span class='line-break'> </span> from Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1700">
<h3><a name="page-1700">Saturday, July 17, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim &amp; Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> worked on the barn shelter<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  Ben went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Strait Stone for oil<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  He went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Gretna for John<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Tenia and Little<span class='line-break'> </span> Christenia.  Josie and<span class='line-break'> </span> I got dinner.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> killed 4 chickens.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie baked a cake.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim &amp; Nellie picked <span class='line-break'> </span> berries this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Nellie caned them.<span class='line-break'> </span> Tonight I made <span class='line-break'> </span> some preserves.<span class='line-break'> </span> This morning got <span class='line-break'> </span> the pears from<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim Thomsons.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1701">
<h3><a name="page-1701">Sunday, July 18, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Rain this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> at two oclock and<span class='line-break'> </span> it is raining a gain<span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  Good all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> John &amp; Tenie and Chris<span class='line-break'> </span> tenia was here.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> carried them home.<span class='line-break'> </span> Evylin went with<span class='line-break'> </span> them.  They got back<span class='line-break'> </span> here at dark.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim Thomson &amp; family<span class='line-break'> </span> come to see us <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> and family was <span class='line-break'> </span> here this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and I got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Johnson &amp; Mollie<span class='line-break'> </span> come this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mollie eat dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> with us.<span class='line-break'> </span> We had two water<span class='line-break'> </span> mellons this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben bought them.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9:15 oclock  </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1702">
<h3><a name="page-1702">Monday, July 19, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Rain this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> The boys toped some<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco.  Josie &amp; I got<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.  Nell worked <span class='line-break'> </span> on Evylins hat this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  I gathered <span class='line-break'> </span> one gallon of berries.<span class='line-break'> </span> Hattie Gilbert<span class='line-break'> </span> brought 6 gallons.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and I caned<span class='line-break'> </span> them.  Carrie and<span class='line-break'> </span> the childrens come<span class='line-break'> </span> down here.  Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> was not at home<span class='line-break'> </span> and there was a <span class='line-break'> </span> bad looking cloud.<span class='line-break'> </span> Evylin &amp; Henry went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Renan this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate Harvey was <span class='line-break'> </span> at Carries this evening.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1703">
<h3><a name="page-1703">Tuesday, July 20, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Rain last<span class='line-break'> </span> night.  Ben &amp; Jim toped<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco this evening.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> helped rais a shed to Doss s [?]<span class='line-break'> </span> barn.  Josie got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> She fried chicken.  Had <span class='line-break'> </span> corn &amp; butter beans.  The <span class='line-break'> </span> first mess this year.<span class='line-break'> </span> I gathered some<span class='line-break'> </span> berries.  Nellie gathered<span class='line-break'> </span> berries.  We caned some<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; preserved some.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Carries<span class='line-break'> </span> a while.  Evylin &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> Virginia is here tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Charles brought<span class='line-break'> </span> them here.<span class='line-break'> </span> They are in the parlor<span class='line-break'> </span> playing on the piano.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1704">
<h3><a name="page-1704">Wednesday, July 21, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Rain this morning but not<span class='line-break'> </span> much.  Jim and Ben has<span class='line-break'> </span> got some tobacco sticks [?]<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and I got dinner.  We<span class='line-break'> </span> had our first tomatoes.<span class='line-break'> </span> I cooked some plant<span class='line-break'> </span> bed salit to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> We all enjoyed it very<span class='line-break'> </span> much.  Josie has bin<span class='line-break'> </span> complaining all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Virginia went home<span class='line-break'> </span> from here this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Hattie brough some<span class='line-break'> </span> berries this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and I caned<span class='line-break'> </span> them.  Nellie made<span class='line-break'> </span> some preserves this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  I fell and <span class='line-break'> </span> hurt my self<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1705">
<h3><a name="page-1705">Thursday, July 22, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Foggy this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> but no rain today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; Jim got sticks<span class='line-break'> </span> a gain today.  Josie got<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.  Charles &amp; Irvin<span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey come here on a<span class='line-break'> </span> car.  Charles worked <span class='line-break'> </span> on it all the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Would not stay to dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Charles come this eve<span class='line-break'> </span> and carried Evylin<span class='line-break'> </span> to Mr Moses to a party.<span class='line-break'> </span> I planted some pepper<span class='line-break'> </span> plants and peas.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  Carrie was<span class='line-break'> </span> canning berries.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I picked a bucketful<span class='line-break'> </span> and canned them.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1706">
<h3><a name="page-1706">Friday, July 23, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at home all day.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Marvin went to Brook<span class='line-break'> </span> neal.  Have not come<span class='line-break'> </span> home yet.  Nellie &amp; Evylin<span class='line-break'> </span> went home.  Charles Harvey<span class='line-break'> </span> carried them.  Josie baked<span class='line-break'> </span> a cake for Nellie this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  Josie got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Josie and <span class='line-break'> </span> I washed some.<span class='line-break'> </span> Christenia Reynols and <span class='line-break'> </span> her mother come to Marvins.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and I went up <span class='line-break'> </span> there a few minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span> Eva Smith is sick.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie washed.  Hattie<span class='line-break'> </span> Gilbert helped her.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1707">
<h3><a name="page-1707">Saturday, July 24, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day and very<span class='line-break'> </span> warm.  To night we<span class='line-break'> </span> have a hard rain.  Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Ben topped tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> nearly all day.  Late<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Josie and three<span class='line-break'> </span> children went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim Powers.  Said they<span class='line-break'> </span> would come home<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight but they wont<span class='line-break'> </span> on acount of rain.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie washed some<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning &amp; got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Corn, butter beans, potato, baked pies.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin let Rees take me to<span class='line-break'> </span> White Falls.  I caught <span class='line-break'> </span> 34 fish.  I eat dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> at Carries.  Eva is sick.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1708">
<h3><a name="page-1708">Sunday, July 25, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben &amp; Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> and children got home about<span class='line-break'> </span> dark.  Jim got huckle<span class='line-break'> </span> berries enough to make<span class='line-break'> </span> three pies.  I made them.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> a while this evening.  Kate<span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey was there.  Reese<span class='line-break'> </span> carried her home.  Carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> and all the children<span class='line-break'> </span> and I went with her.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim has staid around <span class='line-break'> </span> home all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; family and Mrs<span class='line-break'> </span> Car &amp; Mrs Power went to Mr Role<span class='line-break'> </span> Hubards to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1709">
<h3><a name="page-1709">Monday, July 26, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good cool day.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Jim topped tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got dinner.  I churned<span class='line-break'> </span> and cut the cucumber<span class='line-break'> </span> for pickle.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie commenced her<span class='line-break'> </span> a dress and went <span class='line-break'> </span> to Carries a little <span class='line-break'> </span> while.  I picked a<span class='line-break'> </span> bucket of baries.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Mr Owens.<span class='line-break'> </span> His baby is sick.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am sorrie for them &amp; the baby.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> dont know what<span class='line-break'> </span> is the matter with<span class='line-break'> </span> him.  Marvin went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Strait Stone<span class='line-break'> </span> to preaching.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1710">
<h3><a name="page-1710">Tuesday, July 27, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good cool day.  Ben &amp; Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> topped tobacco all the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> At twelve they went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Mt Airy and to Barbers.<span class='line-break'> </span> Bought 100 pounds of <span class='line-break'> </span> sugar and paid 28<span class='line-break'> </span> dollars for it.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Hattie brought<span class='line-break'> </span> some berries.  I caned<span class='line-break'> </span> them.  Mr Carter &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> wife &amp; girl and Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> Hunt Hargrove &amp; Miss<span class='line-break'> </span> Alice Hubbard come<span class='line-break'> </span> here a few minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad they<span class='line-break'> </span> they come.  They went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Strait Stone to<span class='line-break'> </span> preaching.  Josie and<span class='line-break'> </span> the children and I <span class='line-break'> </span> went to Carries.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1711">
<h3><a name="page-1711">Wednesday, July 28, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim &amp; Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> topped tobacco all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie ironed some this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning and got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> I milked &amp; churned &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> cut the cucumbers<span class='line-break'> </span> for pickle.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> we all went to <span class='line-break'> </span> Marvins.  He had bin <span class='line-break'> </span> to Altavista and<span class='line-break'> </span> brought ice.  We had<span class='line-break'> </span> all the cream that<span class='line-break'> </span> we could eat.<span class='line-break'> </span> We certainly did<span class='line-break'> </span> enjoy it.  To night<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin and Carrie has<span class='line-break'> </span> gone to preaching.  To<span class='line-break'> </span> night William [?]<span class='line-break'> </span> is keeping the children.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1712">
<h3><a name="page-1712">Thursday, July 29, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben &amp; Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> worked in their tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> until noon then they<span class='line-break'> </span> sowed a turnip patch<span class='line-break'> </span> and worked in tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> some more.  Josie got dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> and ironed.  Reese carried<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry and I fishing.<span class='line-break'> </span> We caught several<span class='line-break'> </span> fish.  I could not dig <span class='line-break'> </span> for bait.  Josie got them <span class='line-break'> </span> for me.  I wore<span class='line-break'> </span> her nice watch the <span class='line-break'> </span> first one that I ever<span class='line-break'> </span> wore.  Bettie Haley<span class='line-break'> </span> washed here today.<span class='line-break'> </span> She had a boy to help<span class='line-break'> </span> her.  I went to Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> Owens this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry has bin sick all day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1713">
<h3><a name="page-1713">Friday, July 30, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men<span class='line-break'> </span> folks pulled leaves.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; Jim, Owen and<span class='line-break'> </span> boys.  Marvin &amp; William,<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry, Reese, and Elic [?]<span class='line-break'> </span> filled a house and<span class='line-break'> </span> pulled some for another.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie ironed most<span class='line-break'> </span> of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie &amp; the children went<span class='line-break'> </span> to meeting.  Reese<span class='line-break'> </span> drives the car.<span class='line-break'> </span> They come down<span class='line-break'> </span> here a little while.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have jobed a <span class='line-break'> </span> round as usual.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1714">
<h3><a name="page-1714">Saturday, July 31, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  They pulled<span class='line-break'> </span> a house full of tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  Marvin &amp; Carrie, Paul <span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Roy went to the [?]<span class='line-break'> </span> at Camp Branch.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> all eat dinner with us.<span class='line-break'> </span> We were glad to have<span class='line-break'> </span> them.  Kate Harvey<span class='line-break'> </span> come down a while<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna and Mabel<span class='line-break'> </span> caught a fall<span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  Did not <span class='line-break'> </span> hurt them very <span class='line-break'> </span> much.<span class='line-break'> </span> 8:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1715">
<h3><a name="page-1715">Memorandum (vi)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Oh lord remember<span class='line-break'> </span> all of us is<span class='line-break'> </span> my prayer for<span class='line-break'> </span> Christ sake amen</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1716">
<h3><a name="page-1716">Sunday, August  1, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Rain this evening.  Jim staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at the barn most of the <span class='line-break'> </span> day.  Ben &amp; Charley<span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey worked on Bens<span class='line-break'> </span> car all the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening I went<span class='line-break'> </span> with Marvin &amp; Carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> to Strait Stone Church.<span class='line-break'> </span> Heard Mr Padget<span class='line-break'> </span> preach.  They had a hand<span class='line-break'> </span> stakein [?] with the new<span class='line-break'> </span> members.  It rained<span class='line-break'> </span> while we were there.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin got stuck<span class='line-break'> </span> in the mud.  Several<span class='line-break'> </span> helped him out.  Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> kept Carries children.<span class='line-break'> </span> I know among them <span class='line-break'> </span> they gave her a time.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1717">
<h3><a name="page-1717">Monday, August  2, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben worked<span class='line-break'> </span> on his car the most of<span class='line-break'> </span> the day.  Jim fired tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  Josie got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got the breakfast and<span class='line-break'> </span> milked the cows and<span class='line-break'> </span> churned.  I cut cucumber<span class='line-break'> </span> and put them in brine.<span class='line-break'> </span> I gathered some butter <span class='line-break'> </span> beans and corn for dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening I went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Union Grove to preaching.<span class='line-break'> </span> Reese carried his mother<span class='line-break'> </span> and I.  When I come<span class='line-break'> </span> home I milked the cows<span class='line-break'> </span> and eat supper and<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Marvins.  He<span class='line-break'> </span> carried me and Carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> to Mr Allens to preaching.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1718">
<h3><a name="page-1718">Tuesday, August  3, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim worked<span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  Ben went <span class='line-break'> </span> with me to Chatham.<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate Harvey went with<span class='line-break'> </span> us.  We eat dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> at Nellies.  Nellie and<span class='line-break'> </span> Evylin come home<span class='line-break'> </span> with us.  Josie staid<span class='line-break'> </span> and got dinner.  This<span class='line-break'> </span> evening Josie and<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie went to see <span class='line-break'> </span> Mollie.  They walked<span class='line-break'> </span> up there.  Reese met<span class='line-break'> </span> them with the car<span class='line-break'> </span> and brought them<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  Marvin commenced<span class='line-break'> </span> to pull leaves today.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1719">
<h3><a name="page-1719">Wednesday, August  4, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> pulled leaves.  Jim &amp; Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Owen helped him.<span class='line-break'> </span> Reese carried Nell &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie to Jim Thomsons.<span class='line-break'> </span> They got a bout two<span class='line-break'> </span> bushels of peaches.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Nellie<span class='line-break'> </span> and I peeled them.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie helped in<span class='line-break'> </span> the tobacco all the <span class='line-break'> </span> evening or until they<span class='line-break'> </span> finished.  Christenia<span class='line-break'> </span> Reynols &amp; Doris Brum<span class='line-break'> </span> come a little while.<span class='line-break'> </span> They got some <span class='line-break'> </span> tomatoes.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1720">
<h3><a name="page-1720">Thursday, August  5, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A rainy day.  The boys<span class='line-break'> </span> pulled some leaves and<span class='line-break'> </span> got wet.  Josie went to see<span class='line-break'> </span> the Owen baby.  This <span class='line-break'> </span> morning Nellie made<span class='line-break'> </span> some preserves.  I caned<span class='line-break'> </span> three cans of peaches<span class='line-break'> </span> and made some preserves.<span class='line-break'> </span> Evylin went to see<span class='line-break'> </span> Virginia this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna went to Marvins <span class='line-break'> </span> and got some butter<span class='line-break'> </span> and meal.<span class='line-break'> </span> We had snaps and corn<span class='line-break'> </span> and stewed &amp; raw<span class='line-break'> </span> tomatoes, peaches and <span class='line-break'> </span> cream for dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> I do hope it is going<span class='line-break'> </span> to clear up now.<span class='line-break'> </span> 8:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1721">
<h3><a name="page-1721">Friday, August  6, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy morning<span class='line-break'> </span> but no rain.  The<span class='line-break'> </span> men folks pulled<span class='line-break'> </span> some leaves and finished<span class='line-break'> </span> the house that they had<span class='line-break'> </span> commenced on.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie &amp; I got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Evylin come from<span class='line-break'> </span> Kates.  Kate come<span class='line-break'> </span> to Carries and helped<span class='line-break'> </span> her on her dress.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went up there<span class='line-break'> </span> a little while this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening and come<span class='line-break'> </span> home through Bens<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco.  I have<span class='line-break'> </span> had the tooth ache<span class='line-break'> </span> all the evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1722">
<h3><a name="page-1722">Saturday, August  7, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men folks<span class='line-break'> </span> suckered tobacco.  Ben <span class='line-break'> </span> went to Mr Vaugns [?]<span class='line-break'> </span> to get a flue.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and I got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Nellie and Evylin<span class='line-break'> </span> started home.  Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> carried them to Altavista.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  She was<span class='line-break'> </span> washing.  Kate Harvey<span class='line-break'> </span> and Hattie Gilbert<span class='line-break'> </span> was helping her.<span class='line-break'> </span> We ironed some<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1723">
<h3><a name="page-1723">Sunday, August  8, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at the barn most of the <span class='line-break'> </span> day.  Ben went to George<span class='line-break'> </span> Blairs and helped Earl<span class='line-break'> </span> Bennett work on his car.<span class='line-break'> </span> John Emerson and Sarah<span class='line-break'> </span> and four of their<span class='line-break'> </span> children come here<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  I was glad <span class='line-break'> </span> to see them.<span class='line-break'> </span> Hugh Brumfield come<span class='line-break'> </span> to see Henry today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie &amp; the children<span class='line-break'> </span> and I went to Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> late this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> The children<span class='line-break'> </span> tried them selves.<span class='line-break'> </span> 8:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1724">
<h3><a name="page-1724">Monday, August  9, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A rainy day most<span class='line-break'> </span> of the day.  Ben &amp; Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> suckered tobacco a while.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim worked on his tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben kept up fire/fine [?] in<span class='line-break'> </span> the barn.  Josie got<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.  I made a few<span class='line-break'> </span> preserves of peaches<span class='line-break'> </span> that growed here. <span class='line-break'> </span> Pulled green[s] [?]<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie come a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes for some soda.<span class='line-break'> </span> We owed her a pound.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie is washing<span class='line-break'> </span> dishes now.  The baby<span class='line-break'> </span> is a sleep.  Kate come<span class='line-break'> </span> to Carries to day<span class='line-break'> </span> to see about some<span class='line-break'> </span> sowing.<span class='line-break'> </span> 8:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1725">
<h3><a name="page-1725">Tuesday, August 10, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Cloudy most of the day<span class='line-break'> </span> and a hard rain this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  The men worked<span class='line-break'> </span> in the tobacco when they<span class='line-break'> </span> could work.  Josie got<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.  I washed<span class='line-break'> </span> dishes and churned.<span class='line-break'> </span> I dressed three<span class='line-break'> </span> chickens this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> The association commence<span class='line-break'> </span> at Ricevill today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Cordie Blair come<span class='line-break'> </span> to see us this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> She brough some<span class='line-break'> </span> beautiful dalahs<span class='line-break'> </span> all colors.  I was <span class='line-break'> </span> very glad that she<span class='line-break'> </span> come.<span class='line-break'> </span> 8:35 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1726">
<h3><a name="page-1726">Wednesday, August 11, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Rain this evening.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Jim [&amp;]Henry suckered<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco.  Josie and three<span class='line-break'> </span> children and went <span class='line-break'> </span> to Ricevill to the<span class='line-break'> </span> assosiation.  Marvin &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> his family went.<span class='line-break'> </span> Reese drove Bens<span class='line-break'> </span> car.  There was a <span class='line-break'> </span> big crowd there<span class='line-break'> </span> and a plenty to <span class='line-break'> </span> eat.  Every one seem<span class='line-break'> </span> to have a good<span class='line-break'> </span> time.  I met a lot <span class='line-break'> </span> of old friends.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim &amp; Ben &amp; Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> eat cold dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1727">
<h3><a name="page-1727">Thursday, August 12, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  It did not<span class='line-break'> </span> rain today here.  It rained<span class='line-break'> </span> in sight.   The men folks<span class='line-break'> </span> worked on their tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got dinner.  She<span class='line-break'> </span> cooked snaps and butter<span class='line-break'> </span> beans.  Reese carried<span class='line-break'> </span> me to Johnson Reynols<span class='line-break'> </span> to get some peaches.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got enough to<span class='line-break'> </span> put up two gallons.<span class='line-break'> </span> We had peaches and<span class='line-break'> </span> cream for dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie gathered some<span class='line-break'> </span> beans.  I helped a little.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to the sweet<span class='line-break'> </span> potato patch and got<span class='line-break'> </span> a few potatoes.<span class='line-break'> </span> I intend makein pies.<span class='line-break'> </span> 8:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1728">
<h3><a name="page-1728">Friday, August 13, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Rain tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> The men cut a caneing<span class='line-break'> </span> of tobacco for Mr Owens<span class='line-break'> </span> and commenced to <span class='line-break'> </span> pull one for Jim.<span class='line-break'> </span> Owen went to the <span class='line-break'> </span> mill.  Got two barrel<span class='line-break'> </span> of flour.  Betty Haley<span class='line-break'> </span> washed here to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Berger was <span class='line-break'> </span> buried today.  Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> and Carrie went to<span class='line-break'> </span> the buriel.  Roy staid<span class='line-break'> </span> here.  Maggie Bar[?]<span class='line-break'> </span> and 4 of the <span class='line-break'> </span> children come<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> carried them<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  I was glad<span class='line-break'> </span> for him to take them.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1729">
<h3><a name="page-1729">Saturday, August 14, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day and<span class='line-break'> </span> rain this evening.  The<span class='line-break'> </span> men pulled leaves.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got dinner &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> caned tomatoes.  I<span class='line-break'> </span> made some jellie.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie ironed some.<span class='line-break'> </span> Earl Bennett come<span class='line-break'> </span> over here a while.<span class='line-break'> </span> He is at George<span class='line-break'> </span> Blairs tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> I killed two <span class='line-break'> </span> chickens to cook<span class='line-break'> </span> in the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie made some<span class='line-break'> </span> nice pies.  I intend<span class='line-break'> </span> going to Richmond to<span class='line-break'> </span> morrow if nothing<span class='line-break'> </span> happens to hinder.<span class='line-break'> </span> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1730">
<h3><a name="page-1730">Sunday, August 15, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Rain to<span class='line-break'> </span> night.  Ben brought<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate and I to Long<span class='line-break'> </span> Island.  We made the<span class='line-break'> </span> trip ok.  John was<span class='line-break'> </span> with us as far as<span class='line-break'> </span> Altavista then Oscar<span class='line-break'> </span> Booker was with us<span class='line-break'> </span> as far as Richmond.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr Louvan [?] brought<span class='line-break'> </span> us to Wills.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> had a nice supper.<span class='line-break'> </span> Found them all <span class='line-break'> </span> well.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1731">
<h3><a name="page-1731">Monday, August 16, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  It has<span class='line-break'> </span> not rained here yet<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  Will come<span class='line-break'> </span> home today. Effie and<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate and I went<span class='line-break'> </span> down town this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I enjoy going but<span class='line-break'> </span> it was very hot.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1732">
<h3><a name="page-1732">Tuesday, August 17, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very hot day and<span class='line-break'> </span> a hard cloud tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate staid here<span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  Julia B<span class='line-break'> </span> and I went to town.<span class='line-break'> </span> I bought a hand<span class='line-break'> </span> pocket. [?]<span class='line-break'> </span> Willie Brumfield<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Norfolk<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  Said he<span class='line-break'> </span> would come home<span class='line-break'> </span> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span> Effie had her<span class='line-break'> </span> washing done to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Effie had rools for<span class='line-break'> </span> supper.  I<span class='line-break'> </span> have not felt so well<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  Hope I will feel<span class='line-break'> </span> better by morning.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1733">
<h3><a name="page-1733">Wednesday, August 18, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Effie &amp; the <span class='line-break'> </span> children, Kate and<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Holly<span class='line-break'> </span> Wood Cemetry.<span class='line-break'> </span> We carried our<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner and eat<span class='line-break'> </span> down there.<span class='line-break'> </span> We have had a <span class='line-break'> </span> hard rain &amp; thunder<span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  Effie &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate caned<span class='line-break'> </span> some tomatoes this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Willie Brumfield<span class='line-break'> </span> come home from<span class='line-break'> </span> Norfolk to day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1734">
<h3><a name="page-1734">Thursday, August 19, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A rainy day.  We<span class='line-break'> </span> Will &amp; Kate and<span class='line-break'> </span> Effie [and] I<span class='line-break'> </span> come to Washington.<span class='line-break'> </span> We got dinner &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> rode a round a lot.<span class='line-break'> </span> Saw beautiful <span class='line-break'> </span> flowers &amp; building.<span class='line-break'> </span> Staid at the Driscoll<span class='line-break'> </span> Hotel.  Paid two $2:00<span class='line-break'> </span> a peice for a bed<span class='line-break'> </span> and 70 cts for break[fast].<span class='line-break'> </span> I am wasting on the<span class='line-break'> </span> 20.00.  We went to a <span class='line-break'> </span> picture show last<span class='line-break'> </span> night.  Walked a<span class='line-break'> </span> bout ten blocks.<span class='line-break'> </span> I enjoyed some of <span class='line-break'> </span> it very much.<span class='line-break'> </span> Was tired last night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1735">
<h3><a name="page-1735">Friday, August 20, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very rainy morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> We are in Washington.<span class='line-break'> </span> Willie went to Alexes [?]<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  He come<span class='line-break'> </span> back and we walked<span class='line-break'> </span> to the monument.<span class='line-break'> </span> Went up in the elevator.<span class='line-break'> </span> I did not want to go<span class='line-break'> </span> but am glad that I <span class='line-break'> </span> did.  We come to<span class='line-break'> </span> Richmond in the <span class='line-break'> </span> night.  Had a good <span class='line-break'> </span> trip.  Got to Richmond<span class='line-break'> </span> a bout midnight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Effies children was<span class='line-break'> </span> all a sleep.<span class='line-break'> </span> This is wrote on the<span class='line-break'> </span> morning of the 21st.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1736">
<h3><a name="page-1736">Saturday, August 21, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>We are in Richmond<span class='line-break'> </span> and it is raining.<span class='line-break'> </span> We went to capital<span class='line-break'> </span> and looked a round<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Went <span class='line-break'> </span> to see the market.<span class='line-break'> </span> There is every thing<span class='line-break'> </span> to eat that you<span class='line-break'> </span> can think of.<span class='line-break'> </span> Miss Irene Dyer<span class='line-break'> </span> come to Richmond<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1737">
<h3><a name="page-1737">Sunday, August 22, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Kate<span class='line-break'> </span> and I come home<span class='line-break'> </span> from Richmond to<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  Willie come<span class='line-break'> </span> with us.  We come<span class='line-break'> </span> home on the Virginian.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; Edna and <span class='line-break'> </span> Franklin met us<span class='line-break'> </span> at Long Island.<span class='line-break'> </span> Found all well<span class='line-break'> </span> as ususal.  The boys<span class='line-break'> </span> is curing tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span> They had plenty of<span class='line-break'> </span> water mellons.<span class='line-break'> </span> Nellie and Evylin<span class='line-break'> </span> are here.
