Josie &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> Nell had caned <span class='line-break'> </span> a lot of tomatoes.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1738">
<h3><a name="page-1738">Monday, August 23, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy bad day.<span class='line-break'> </span> The boys suckered<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco most of the<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  Nellie caned<span class='line-break'> </span> some tomatoes.  Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> helped her some.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Nellie<span class='line-break'> </span> and Josie picked <span class='line-break'> </span> beans.  I helped<span class='line-break'> </span> some.  Ben yoked<span class='line-break'> </span> the spotted heifer.<span class='line-break'> </span> She kept getting<span class='line-break'> </span> in the corn.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> went to Carries<span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  Kate &amp; Virginia<span class='line-break'> </span> was there.  I am<span class='line-break'> </span> suffering with my<span class='line-break'> </span> leg tonight.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1739">
<h3><a name="page-1739">Tuesday, August 24, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  No rain.<span class='line-break'> </span> The men folks cut<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco all day.  Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> staid at the barn<span class='line-break'> </span> all day and kept <span class='line-break'> </span> up the fires.<span class='line-break'> </span> Nellie caned some<span class='line-break'> </span> tomatoes this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> and made preserves<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening and<span class='line-break'> </span> picked some beans.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got the dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie gathered the snaps<span class='line-break'> </span> and corn.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> I gathered a few <span class='line-break'> </span> beans and got<span class='line-break'> </span> some muskmellon<span class='line-break'> </span> and tomatoes.<span class='line-break'> </span> Earl Bennett eat dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> with us today.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1740">
<h3><a name="page-1740">Wednesday, August 25, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The<span class='line-break'> </span> men worked on the<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben carried Nellie<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Evylin home.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie &amp; Mabel went with them.<span class='line-break'> </span> They got home<span class='line-break'> </span> a bout dark.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> I helped Nell<span class='line-break'> </span> pick beans.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Carries<span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span> I gathered some musk mellons.<span class='line-break'> </span> I suckered<span class='line-break'> </span> a little tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1741">
<h3><a name="page-1741">Thursday, August 26, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men<span class='line-break'> </span> folks suckered<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco to day.  Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> and I got dinner.  Bettie<span class='line-break'> </span> Hayley washed here.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr Mcraye come to<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  I went to<span class='line-break'> </span> George Blairs this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  Denia and<span class='line-break'> </span> the girls were busy<span class='line-break'> </span> mending.  Kate <span class='line-break'> </span> and Charles Harvey<span class='line-break'> </span> come to Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> and got a lot of<span class='line-break'> </span> matoes.  Josie gathered<span class='line-break'> </span> a lot of tomatoes<span class='line-break'> </span> and picked up apples<span class='line-break'> </span> for the hogs.  Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> has gone to the barn.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry has gone with him.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1742">
<h3><a name="page-1742">Friday, August 27, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Rain tonight.  The men<span class='line-break'> </span> cut tobacco all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; Owen will stay<span class='line-break'> </span> at the barn.  Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> caned some tomatoes<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning and<span class='line-break'> </span> made preserves<span class='line-break'> </span> and catchsup.<span class='line-break'> </span> She got most of the<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.  I milked and<span class='line-break'> </span> churned and kept<span class='line-break'> </span> busy most of the <span class='line-break'> </span> day.  Miss Willie<span class='line-break'> </span> Wooding come a <span class='line-break'> </span> little while.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry &amp; Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> went hunting<span class='line-break'> </span> last night.  Did <span class='line-break'> </span> not catch anything.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1743">
<h3><a name="page-1743">Monday, August 30, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">

They will <span class='line-break'> </span> stay with a barn<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and I washed<span class='line-break'> </span> a big washing<span class='line-break'> </span> and got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening we<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> a little while.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie &amp; Carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> picked some snaps.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and I strung<span class='line-break'> </span> ours to night.</p>
</div>

<br />
<div id="page-1744">
<h3><a name="page-1744">Tuesday, August 31, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Driscoll Hotel [written in a different ink from the rest of the entry]<span class='line-break'> </span> A good day.  The men<span class='line-break'> </span> folks moved and cut<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco.  Ben finished<span class='line-break'> </span> cutting Bens tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> his crop.  Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> caned nine cans<span class='line-break'> </span> of tomatoes &amp; corn.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie &amp; the<span class='line-break'> </span> three little<span class='line-break'> </span> children come<span class='line-break'> </span> here a little <span class='line-break'> </span> while this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> West Wooding<span class='line-break'> </span> run his car over<span class='line-break'> </span> Bens dog.  She dont<span class='line-break'> </span> eppear to be<span class='line-break'> </span> much hurt.<span class='line-break'> </span> They will stay with<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco to night.</p>
</div>

<div id="page-1745">
<h3><a name="page-1745">Memorandum (vii)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>From Long Island<span class='line-break'> </span> to Alberta $2:69<span class='line-break'> </span> from Alberta to Richmond<span class='line-break'> </span> $1:98<span class='line-break'> </span> From Washington<span class='line-break'> </span> to Richmond $3:78</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1746">
<h3><a name="page-1746">Wednesday, September  1, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">

Ben fired tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span> Chanler Harvey and<span class='line-break'> </span> Dodson Bailiss come<span class='line-break'> </span> to the barn.  Henry B and<span class='line-break'> </span> Cordie B come a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie ironed some.<span class='line-break'> </span> Bettie Haley washed<span class='line-break'> </span> here today.  Jim brought<span class='line-break'> </span> a barrel of flour <span class='line-break'> </span> from Marvins today.<span class='line-break'> </span> I picked a few<span class='line-break'> </span> butter beans today.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am going to shell some beans<span class='line-break'> </span> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock</p>

<div id="page-1747">
<h3><a name="page-1747">Thursday, September  2, 1920</a></h3>

Johnson brought<span class='line-break'> </span> them &amp; come after<span class='line-break'> </span> them.  Josie and I<span class='line-break'> </span> got dinner.  Kate<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Charles Harvey<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Mr Edmons<span class='line-break'> </span> for peaches.<span class='line-break'> </span> Owens folks went <span class='line-break'> </span> to Strait Stone<span class='line-break'> </span> today.</p>

<div id="page-1748">
<h3><a name="page-1748">Friday, September  3, 1920</a></h3>

Josie fired<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco this morning and<span class='line-break'> </span> picked a basket of beans.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got the dinner.  This <span class='line-break'> </span> evening Josie &amp; Carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> and the little children<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Lee Brumfield.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben carried them<span class='line-break'> </span> and Reese brought<span class='line-break'> </span> them home.  Jack<span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey got home<span class='line-break'> </span> yesterday from Richmond.<span class='line-break'> </span> Charles Harvey and Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield went a <span class='line-break'> </span> round to gather today.<span class='line-break'> </span> The men folks wont<span class='line-break'> </span> have to sit up tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1749">
<h3><a name="page-1749">Saturday, September  4, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men<span class='line-break'> </span> folks moved tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie helped them<span class='line-break'> </span> all the evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got dinner.  She <span class='line-break'> </span> cooked snaps and turnip<span class='line-break'> </span> salit.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to see Mr Owens<span class='line-break'> </span> baby this morning.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> called the Dr to see <span class='line-break'> </span> it.  He is very sick.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to see <span class='line-break'> </span> Sarah Emerson this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  Henry &amp; Hellen<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield went.<span class='line-break'> </span> Reese Smith carried<span class='line-break'> </span> us.  He is a good driver.<span class='line-break'> </span> I eat supper with<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie to night.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim is at the barn tonight.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1750">
<h3><a name="page-1750">Sunday, September  5, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day.  Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> staid at the barn.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> brought a wheel barrow<span class='line-break'> </span> load of water mellons<span class='line-break'> </span> to the house.  I got most<span class='line-break'> </span> of the dinner.  Fried chicken<span class='line-break'> </span> and made coffee and bread.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie baked a cake.<span class='line-break'> </span> Roy Smith was very<span class='line-break'> </span> sick this morning.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> called in the Dr.<span class='line-break'> </span> He is better this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie &amp; the children<span class='line-break'> </span> and I went up there<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim went to the barn <span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1751">
<h3><a name="page-1751">Monday, September  6, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men<span class='line-break'> </span> folks rehung two<span class='line-break'> </span> cureings of tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> and moved them and<span class='line-break'> </span> hauled some sticks.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel has bin sick <span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  They carried<span class='line-break'> </span> her to the Dr to <span class='line-break'> </span> night.  I hope she<span class='line-break'> </span> may be better by <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  I got<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner and went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Marvins a few <span class='line-break'> </span> minutes.  I gathered<span class='line-break'> </span> some snaps and<span class='line-break'> </span> dried beans and<span class='line-break'> </span> butter beans.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim has gone to<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvins to night.</p>

<br />
<div id="page-1752">
<h3><a name="page-1752">Tuesday, September  7, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">

Mabel <span class='line-break'> </span> is very sick.  Dr. Owen<span class='line-break'> </span> was at Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> to see Roy.  Josie <span class='line-break'> </span> carried the baby<span class='line-break'> </span> to see him.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> and picked some <span class='line-break'> </span> beans.<span class='line-break'> </span> Dr. Owen brought<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie &amp; the children<span class='line-break'> </span> home and I was <span class='line-break'> </span> glad.<span class='line-break'> </span> None of the boys<span class='line-break'> </span> will have to stay<span class='line-break'> </span> at the barn.</p>
</div>

<br />
<div id="page-1753">
<h3><a name="page-1753">Wednesday, September  8, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Cloudy <span class='line-break'> </span> tonight and looks like<span class='line-break'> </span> rain.  The men folks cut<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco and moved some<span class='line-break'> </span> to the grainry.  Jim and <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben has gone to mowing.<span class='line-break'> </span> The baby is sick yet.<span class='line-break'> </span> We hope she is better<span class='line-break'> </span> than she was last night.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have done the work<span class='line-break'> </span> at the kitchen today.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes to<span class='line-break'> </span> day then picked some<span class='line-break'> </span> peas.  Roy is better.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin &amp; William<span class='line-break'> </span> was cutting tobacco.</p>

<div id="page-1754">
<h3><a name="page-1754">Thursday, September  9, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day.  No rain.<span class='line-break'> </span> They men cut a house<span class='line-break'> </span> of tobacco for Jim.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim &amp; Ben went to the <span class='line-break'> </span> barn.  Ben &amp; Josie went<span class='line-break'> </span> to carrie Mabel to<span class='line-break'> </span> the Dr this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> She is mightily bad<span class='line-break'> </span> off some way.  She<span class='line-break'> </span> cries nearly all the <span class='line-break'> </span> time she is awake.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I am sorry for her and<span class='line-break'> </span> all the rest of us.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got dinner cooked.<span class='line-break'> </span> Peas and chicken.<span class='line-break'> </span> Had a dish of snaps.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have bin at <span class='line-break'> </span> home all day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1755">
<h3><a name="page-1755">Friday, September 10, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">

I handed<span class='line-break'> </span> leaves this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> William Gilbert helped<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Betty Haley washed today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel is right much<span class='line-break'> </span> better off to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Owens baby is sick.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  Ben has<span class='line-break'> </span> bin at the barn<span class='line-break'> </span> today and tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry Blair and<span class='line-break'> </span> Charles Harvey<span class='line-break'> </span> come to the barn<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> 8:30 oclock</p>

<div id="page-1756">
<h3><a name="page-1756">Saturday, September 11, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">

Got home after<span class='line-break'> </span> dark.  Mr Owen finished<span class='line-break'> </span> fireing two cureings.<span class='line-break'> </span> To night Jim will stay <span class='line-break'> </span> with his barn tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie &amp; Franklin<span class='line-break'> </span> are both sick tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Reynols to<span class='line-break'> </span> day to see Julia.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> had a lot of company<span class='line-break'> </span> mostly their own folks.<span class='line-break'> </span> Robert brought me<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  I went by <span class='line-break'> </span> Marvins.  Carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> was finishing washing.<span class='line-break'> </span> I pittie the young<span class='line-break'> </span> house keepers.</p>

<div id="page-1757">
<h3><a name="page-1757">Sunday, September 12, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">

Jim staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at the barn all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and I got<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; family and<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> Powers.  Had a pleasant<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  Come home.<span class='line-break'> </span> I milked.  Josie got<span class='line-break'> </span> supper.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Marvin went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Strait Stone.  Thought<span class='line-break'> </span> there would be<span class='line-break'> </span> preaching.  There was<span class='line-break'> </span> none.<span class='line-break'> </span> 8 oclock</p>

<div id="page-1758">
<h3><a name="page-1758">Monday, September 13, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
