<div id="page-1759">
<h3><a name="page-1759">Tuesday, September 14, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim and<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben commence to cut<span class='line-break'> </span> corn.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to White<span class='line-break'> </span> Falls.  Reese Smith<span class='line-break'> </span> carried me &amp; Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> on the machine.<span class='line-break'> </span> I did not catch <span class='line-break'> </span> many fish.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Bettie Haley come<span class='line-break'> </span> and ironed for Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie Smith<span class='line-break'> </span> come down and<span class='line-break'> </span> got a few aples.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; Henry &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> Reese has gone<span class='line-break'> </span> hunting to night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1760">
<h3><a name="page-1760">Wednesday, September 15, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and Henry helped<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr Owen finish cutting<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco.  Jim has gone<span class='line-break'> </span> to Marvins to night.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and I got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie put some apples<span class='line-break'> </span> out to dry to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> I picked some beans<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Charles<span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey stoped in a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mollie &amp; Christenia<span class='line-break'> </span> Reynols come this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  I was<span class='line-break'> </span> glad that they<span class='line-break'> </span> come.  Josie is in<span class='line-break'> </span> the parlor playing<span class='line-break'> </span> on the piano.<span class='line-break'> </span> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1761">
<h3><a name="page-1761">Thursday, September 16, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Clouds<span class='line-break'> </span> a round but no rain here.<span class='line-break'> </span> The men folks moved<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben has gone to Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got dinner.  She<span class='line-break'> </span> cooked turnip salit.<span class='line-break'> </span> We did enjoy it.<span class='line-break'> </span> I picked beans<span class='line-break'> </span> most of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Went to Carries<span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes<span class='line-break'> </span> and to the pea patch.<span class='line-break'> </span> Picked a basket<span class='line-break'> </span> full and what I<span class='line-break'> </span> could cram in my apron.  Josie has a<span class='line-break'> </span> colde and cough.<span class='line-break'> </span> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1762">
<h3><a name="page-1762">Friday, September 17, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> fired tobacco.  Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Chatham.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin carried him<span class='line-break'> </span> a part of the way.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie ironed some<span class='line-break'> </span> and got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> I picked some peas<span class='line-break'> </span> and killed a chcken<span class='line-break'> </span> and churned.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Hugh<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield and<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry Brumfield and <span class='line-break'> </span> I went to White Falls<span class='line-break'> </span> fishing.  We did not<span class='line-break'> </span> catch many fish.<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate Harvey come<span class='line-break'> </span> while I was<span class='line-break'> </span> gone.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1763">
<h3><a name="page-1763">Saturday, September 18, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> went for Rob<span class='line-break'> </span> Hubbard and family<span class='line-break'> </span> and Mrs Car.<span class='line-break'> </span> Faber Jefferson &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> family and Lizzie<span class='line-break'> </span> Bennett come at<span class='line-break'> </span> dark.  They had<span class='line-break'> </span> supper.  Josie and<span class='line-break'> </span> I got dinner and<span class='line-break'> </span> ironed some.  Reese<span class='line-break'> </span> carried me to White <span class='line-break'> </span> Falls.  Henry went <span class='line-break'> </span> with us.<span class='line-break'> </span> We are a bout<span class='line-break'> </span> ready to go to bed.<span class='line-break'> </span> 11 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1764">
<h3><a name="page-1764">Sunday, September 19, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We had<span class='line-break'> </span> a lot of company<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  Rob Hubbard<span class='line-break'> </span> and family &amp; Mrs. Car[,]<span class='line-break'> </span> Lizzie Bennett &amp; Fabar<span class='line-break'> </span> Jefferson &amp; family.<span class='line-break'> </span> Lee &amp; Hildna come<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> and three children<span class='line-break'> </span> come a little while.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and I got<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.  We cooked<span class='line-break'> </span> snaps and potatoes<span class='line-break'> </span> and chicken.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie had baked a cake.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben carried Rob<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; family home this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Paul &amp; Earl Bennett<span class='line-break'> </span> come and carried Lizzie<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Faber home tonight.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1765">
<h3><a name="page-1765">Monday, September 20, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> tied a few primeings<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  This<span class='line-break'> </span> evening Ben went <span class='line-break'> </span> to Gretna.  This morning<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie &amp; she shelled<span class='line-break'> </span> butter beans.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and I got<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner then we<span class='line-break'> </span> went with Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> to Gretna to meet<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim.  He had bin to<span class='line-break'> </span> Danville.  Tobacco sold<span class='line-break'> </span> low.  The market opened<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  The Renan<span class='line-break'> </span> school opened today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim &amp; Ben has<span class='line-break'> </span> gone to Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1766">
<h3><a name="page-1766">Tuesday, September 21, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben &amp; Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> cut corn in the <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim mowed peas.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben went with<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and I to<span class='line-break'> </span> Long Island.  Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> bought two doz<span class='line-break'> </span> quart fruit jars<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie went to Carries<span class='line-break'> </span> for some patterns<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I stoped<span class='line-break'> </span> there.  Carrie was<span class='line-break'> </span> canning apples.<span class='line-break'> </span> I helped peel some<span class='line-break'> </span> apples.  Come home<span class='line-break'> </span> and cut grass for<span class='line-break'> </span> the cows and milked.<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna is at Mr Woodings<span class='line-break'> </span> to night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1767">
<h3><a name="page-1767">Wednesday, September 22, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Jim cut corn most<span class='line-break'> </span> of the day.  Josie caned<span class='line-break'> </span> tomatoes this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> and gathered some<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening and<span class='line-break'> </span> done a lot of things<span class='line-break'> </span> besides.  I shelled<span class='line-break'> </span> a few beans.<span class='line-break'> </span> The children<span class='line-break'> </span> is well placed <span class='line-break'> </span> with the school.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1768">
<h3><a name="page-1768">Thursday, September 23, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy bad day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Had a hard rain<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening and all<span class='line-break'> </span> the pea hay that was<span class='line-break'> </span> on the place is lying<span class='line-break'> </span> on the ground.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim and Ben tied framings<span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  Josie caned<span class='line-break'> </span> some tomatoes this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning and got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> I shelled some beans<span class='line-break'> </span> and went to <span class='line-break'> </span> Marvins.  Was there<span class='line-break'> </span> when it rained so<span class='line-break'> </span> hard.  Charles Harvey<span class='line-break'> </span> was here this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> listing the property.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carry had made<span class='line-break'> </span> the girls some dresses.<span class='line-break'> </span> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1769">
<h3><a name="page-1769">Friday, September 24, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day.  The <span class='line-break'> </span> boys tied tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got the most<span class='line-break'> </span> of the dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Johnson &amp; Mollie<span class='line-break'> </span> come down here<span class='line-break'> </span> a little while<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Betty Haley washed<span class='line-break'> </span> here today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and the children<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Marvins.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went later on.  I<span class='line-break'> </span> worked a few<span class='line-break'> </span> button holes for <span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben has gone<span class='line-break'> </span> huntting to<span class='line-break'> </span> night.<span class='line-break'> </span> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1770">
<h3><a name="page-1770">Saturday, September 25, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim and<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; Marvin went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Danville to a <span class='line-break'> </span> farmers meeting.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am a fraid it<span class='line-break'> </span> wont do any good.<span class='line-break'> </span> Reese carried me<span class='line-break'> </span> to White Falls fishing.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie ironed most<span class='line-break'> </span> of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim &amp; Ben and Owen<span class='line-break'> </span> and Marvin all<span class='line-break'> </span> went to the meeting<span class='line-break'> </span> in Danville.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie washed and<span class='line-break'> </span> let Reese go<span class='line-break'> </span> with me.<span class='line-break'> </span> Hazel was sick<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  I do hope she<span class='line-break'> </span> will be well tomorow.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1771">
<h3><a name="page-1771">Sunday, September 26, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie staid at home<span class='line-break'> </span> until twelve.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> went to meet Jim.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie stopped at Lees.<span class='line-break'> </span> The children went <span class='line-break'> </span> to Gretna.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie and the <span class='line-break'> </span> children and I<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Tim Benson [?]<span class='line-break'> </span> Ola &amp; Faber Jefferson<span class='line-break'> </span> was there.  Gorden &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> Frances come there.<span class='line-break'> </span> Tim and all of them<span class='line-break'> </span> was very nice to us.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin went to <span class='line-break'> </span> meeting at Strait<span class='line-break'> </span> Stone.<span class='line-break'> </span> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1772">
<h3><a name="page-1772">Monday, September 27, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Rain tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim &amp; Ben cut corn<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> they raked hay and<span class='line-break'> </span> shocked it.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie sowed a little.<span class='line-break'> </span> I commenced dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie finished it.  I dug<span class='line-break'> </span> a basket of potatoes<span class='line-break'> </span> and picked a few<span class='line-break'> </span> beans.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to George<span class='line-break'> </span> Blairs.  The girls<span class='line-break'> </span> was busy as could<span class='line-break'> </span> be.  Denia was at<span class='line-break'> </span> Ren Worshams.<span class='line-break'> </span> I would of bin<span class='line-break'> </span> glad to see her but<span class='line-break'> </span> I thought it might <span class='line-break'> </span> rain.  Jim found 8 little frogs. [?]</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1773">
<h3><a name="page-1773">Tuesday, September 28, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day and<span class='line-break'> </span> rain this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> The men rehung<span class='line-break'> </span> some tobacco this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning and cut<span class='line-break'> </span> some this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie was sick this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  I got the<span class='line-break'> </span> most of the dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie ironed some<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to the water<span class='line-break'> </span> mellon patch and<span class='line-break'> </span> got one water<span class='line-break'> </span> mellon &amp; Josie got<span class='line-break'> </span> two.  I went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvins a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie was busy fixing<span class='line-break'> </span> for Sunday.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1774">
<h3><a name="page-1774">Wednesday, September 29, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day.  Ben <span class='line-break'> </span> and Jim fired tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span> This morning Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> and Josie went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Rob Hubbard.  This <span class='line-break'> </span> evening I went <span class='line-break'> </span> to George Blairs.  George<span class='line-break'> </span> Jr come for me.<span class='line-break'> </span> Letcher Craddock &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> family was there &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> Henry Blair come<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  Ollie Colbert<span class='line-break'> </span> brought him from<span class='line-break'> </span> Gretna.  Claud Anderson [?]<span class='line-break'> </span> was there.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry Brumfield<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Charles Harvey<span class='line-break'> </span> come a few <span class='line-break'> </span> minutes this evening.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1775">
<h3><a name="page-1775">Thursday, September 30, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A rainy day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim and Ben tied<span class='line-break'> </span> primings.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie caned some<span class='line-break'> </span> apples.  I peeled them.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got a snack for<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.  I shelled<span class='line-break'> </span> beans all evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie is very much<span class='line-break'> </span> complaining.  I do<span class='line-break'> </span> hope she will be better <span class='line-break'> </span> soon.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel has bin as<span class='line-break'> </span> frisky as a kitten<span class='line-break'> </span> all day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1776">
<h3><a name="page-1776">Friday, October  1, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Oct first day<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> A good day.  Ben &amp; Jim cut<span class='line-break'> </span> corn all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and I got dinner.  While we were<span class='line-break'> </span> eating dinner Charley Harvey &amp; Lee<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield come.  Josie and I registered<span class='line-break'> </span> and paid taxes.  Josie made Edna a<span class='line-break'> </span> dress.  I picked some peas and went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvins.  To day is Mabels birthday.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1777">
<h3><a name="page-1777">Saturday, October  2, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>2ond day<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben and Jim cut corn<span class='line-break'> </span> until dinner this evening.  Ben carried<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna and I [to] White Falls to fish.<span class='line-break'> </span> This morning I washed a little.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got dinner.  There was a lawn<span class='line-break'> </span> party at Strait Stone this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin and the little boys went.<span class='line-break'> </span> The cream was very nice.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; Henry has gone hunting.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1778">
<h3><a name="page-1778">Sunday, October  3, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Sunday 3rd<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> A good day.  We all staid at home<span class='line-break'> </span> and eat dinner.  Jim rambled around <span class='line-break'> </span> all the evening.  Ben &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> family went to Jim Powers.  I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Mag Brumfields.  I went with Johnson<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Mollie on the car.  Kate Harvey went<span class='line-break'> </span> with us.  We then come to Marvins.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim &amp; Alice &amp; the children was at Marvins.<span class='line-break'> </span> They had ice cream &amp; cake.  We heard<span class='line-break'> </span> today that Alice Wooding &amp; Cap Carter<span class='line-break'> </span> was married.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1779">
<h3><a name="page-1779">Monday, October  4, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>4 day cutting <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> A good day.  Jim and Ben finished<span class='line-break'> </span> cutting corn and shockin it.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben went to Gretna.  I went with<span class='line-break'> </span> him to White Falls.  Caught 19 fish.<span class='line-break'> </span> We were at Mount Airy at dark.<span class='line-break'> </span> Got home OK and Ben has gone hunting.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got dinner.  I picked some<span class='line-break'> </span> peas.  Bettie Haley washed here<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  Josie went to Marvins this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  Owen solde tobacco in Boston<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1780">
<h3><a name="page-1780">Tuesday, October  5, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>5th day Tuesday<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben &amp; Jim gathered <span class='line-break'> </span> some apples and made cider.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got dinner.  I<span class='line-break'> </span> picked peas most of the day.  Went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvins a few minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate Harvey come a little while.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Charley Harvey come<span class='line-break'> </span> and brough our tax receipts.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie sent Mrs Nat Wooding<span class='line-break'> </span> some peppers.  Carrie Smith is<span class='line-break'> </span> very much complaining.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1781">
<h3><a name="page-1781">Wednesday, October  6, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>6 day  Jim gathered apples and made<span class='line-break'> </span> some cider.  Ben went to Long<span class='line-break'> </span> Island for guano.  He<span class='line-break'> </span> bought shoes and put them on the <span class='line-break'> </span> horses him self.  He was gone most<span class='line-break'> </span> of the day.  Josie got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> I picked peas this morning.  This<span class='line-break'> </span> evening I washed a little.  Put<span class='line-break'> </span> out the things that Betty left<span class='line-break'> </span> in the tubs.  I went and dug<span class='line-break'> </span> a basket of sweet potatoes.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1782">
<h3><a name="page-1782">Thursday, October  7, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>7th day  Ben and Jim covered<span class='line-break'> </span> the hog pen and dug the sweet <span class='line-break'> </span> potatoes.  Ben got up the pumpkins.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie ironed and helped get<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.  We cooked beans and<span class='line-break'> </span> pumpkin for dinner.  Josie made<span class='line-break'> </span> Franklin a union suit.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Marvins.  Kate Harvey<span class='line-break'> </span> was there.  Hazel is not well.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> carried her to see the Dr this evening.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1783">
<h3><a name="page-1783">Friday, October  8, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>8th  A good day.  Jim went to<span class='line-break'> </span> the mill at Galveston.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> picked up the sweet<span class='line-break'> </span> potatoes and put them in sacks.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got dinner.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben carried Josie and the baby<span class='line-break'> </span> and Franklin and I to Cedar<span class='line-break'> </span> Forest.  I fished in the Creek.<span class='line-break'> </span> The rest of them went to Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> Powers.  Hazel has been sick all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; Henry gone hunting.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1784">
<h3><a name="page-1784">Saturday, October  9, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>9th  A good day.  Jim and Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> plowed some and hauled<span class='line-break'> </span> up the sweet potatoes.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and I got dinner.  Josie pulled<span class='line-break'> </span> weeds in the yard.  I went to Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes this evening.  Reese and<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry and I went to White Falls.<span class='line-break'> </span> Come by Kates.  She was not at home.<span class='line-break'> </span> Gordon Bennett &amp; Frances come this evening.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1785">
<h3><a name="page-1785">Sunday, October 10, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Sunday 10th  A good day.  We all staid at [home].<span class='line-break'> </span> Gordon &amp; Frances went from here this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  I am very glad<span class='line-break'> </span> that they come.  Josie and I got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> We had cabbage &amp; butter beans<span class='line-break'> </span> and chicken.  Ben &amp; Jim hunted<span class='line-break'> </span> for a dog collar &amp; found it.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin and Reese &amp; Paul went<span class='line-break'> </span> to see Mr and Mrs Taz Wooding.<span class='line-break'> </span> Fond them as well as usual.<span class='line-break'> </span> Bens opossum got a way last night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Johns birthday</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1786">
<h3><a name="page-1786">Monday, October 11, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>11th  A good day.  Ben &amp; Jim plowed<span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  I scalded beans all<span class='line-break'> </span> the morning.  Josie sewed a little and<span class='line-break'> </span> got most of the dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin &amp; Carrie and Kate Harvey<span class='line-break'> </span> and I went to Chatham this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie bought a few things for<span class='line-break'> </span> the children.  Kate a few things<span class='line-break'> </span> and I bought a few things two.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie had Carries children this evening.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1787">
<h3><a name="page-1787">Tuesday, October 12, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>12th  A good day.  Jim plowed all<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  Ben went to Gretna<span class='line-break'> </span> with primeings[?]  Franklin went with<span class='line-break'> </span> him.  Roy Smith went to school<span class='line-break'> </span> to day for his first time.  Josie has<span class='line-break'> </span> bin sick all day.  I got dinner.  I<span class='line-break'> </span> baked a potatoe.  Pumpkins the first this fall.<span class='line-break'> </span> Grace Brumfield and went to Cedar<span class='line-break'> </span> Forest fishing.  Did not have any luck.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1788">
<h3><a name="page-1788">Wednesday, October 13, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>13th  A good day.  Jim &amp; Ben plowed <span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  To night Ben carried<span class='line-break'> </span> Richard Wooding and Miss Smith<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  Mrs Owen brought them here.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got dinner.  Betty Haley washed<span class='line-break'> </span> here to day.  I put the beans in<span class='line-break'> </span> sackes to day.  Mabel fell of the step<span class='line-break'> </span> and hurt her self.  I went to Marvins.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie is so hurt that she let Roy go to school.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1789">
<h3><a name="page-1789">Thursday, October 14, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>14th  A good day.  Ben worked on wheat<span class='line-break'> </span> land all.  Jim tied tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr Cawthorn come to day.  He was here<span class='line-break'> </span> for dinner.  Mr [?] <span class='line-break'> </span> was here to day.  Wanted to sell<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben a truck.  He did not buy.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to George Blairs this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  Denia and Cordie<span class='line-break'> </span> was gone to Rens.  They come home.<span class='line-break'> </span> I had a pleasant evening.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1790">
<h3><a name="page-1790">Friday, October 15, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Friday the 15th  <span class='line-break'> </span> A good day.  Ben worked on wheat land<span class='line-break'> </span> all the morning.  He carried Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> to see the Dr.  She is right sick now.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim stripped tobacoo most of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim and Ben has gone to Renan to<span class='line-break'> </span> a speakin.  I got most of the<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.  One of Willie Mayhews<span class='line-break'> </span> children got burnt very bad<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  I went to Marvins a<span class='line-break'> </span> little while this evening.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1791">
<h3><a name="page-1791">Saturday, October 16, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>10th  A good day.  Jim &amp; Ben plowed until<span class='line-break'> </span> twelve oclock.  This evening Ben carried<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim to Gretna.  Franklin<span class='line-break'> </span> and I went with him.  Lizzie <span class='line-break'> </span> come this evening.  I got my<span class='line-break'> </span> interest on bond today.  Josie is feeling<span class='line-break'> </span> mighty bad today.  Kate was at<span class='line-break'> </span> Carries this evening.  I got dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  Ben has gone hunting<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight with Marvin and<span class='line-break'> </span> Reese.  Henry has a bad colde.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1792">
<h3><a name="page-1792">Sunday, October 17, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>17th Sunday.  A good day.  I got breakfast<span class='line-break'> </span> and milked the cows.  Killed tow chickens<span class='line-break'> </span> then went with Lizzie to George<span class='line-break'> </span> Blairs.  Ben carried us part of the way.<span class='line-break'> </span> There was no one at home but George.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Denia had a good dinner.  Blair [?]<span class='line-break'> </span> has the mumps.  Ben and family went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Jim Powers.  Found them well.<span class='line-break'> </span> I think Josie is feeling some better<span class='line-break'> </span> today  Oh I hope she may soon be<span class='line-break'> </span> well.  Marvin and family was at<span class='line-break'> </span> Lees this evening.  I am glad that they went.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1793">
<h3><a name="page-1793">Monday, October 18, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>18th  A good day.  Ben harrowed on wheat<span class='line-break'> </span> land.  Jim come from Chatham today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and Ben went to Mayhews<span class='line-break'> </span> to see the little boy that<span class='line-break'> </span> is so badly burned.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mollie Reynolds come here a little while.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have staid at home all day<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  I got dinner and ironed<span class='line-break'> </span> some.  Josie baked some nice tea<span class='line-break'> </span> cakes for the chldren to take to<span class='line-break'> </span> school.  Jim and Ben are tying primeings.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1794">
<h3><a name="page-1794">Tuesday, October 19, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>19th  A good day.  Ben went to Gretna<span class='line-break'> </span> for a casket for Roy Mayhew.  He died<span class='line-break'> </span> from a burn.  He was buried <span class='line-break'> </span> at his grandpas burial ground.<span class='line-break'> </span> We were all at the burial.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got dinner.  Ben and Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> went to see Martha Miller.<span class='line-break'> </span> She a greed to come here and<span class='line-break'> </span> stay a while.  Henry went with<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin and Reese &amp; Hugh<span class='line-break'> </span> hunting.  Did not catch anything.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1795">
<h3><a name="page-1795">Wednesday, October 20, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>20th  A good day.  Ben sowed some<span class='line-break'> </span> wheat to day.  Jim worked Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> team and disked land.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie made Franklin a suit.  She<span class='line-break'> </span> is hardly able to go a bout.  I am<span class='line-break'> </span> distressed a bout her.  I was at<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvins a few minutes this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Virginia Wooding and Ula Mayhew<span class='line-break'> </span> is here tonight from school.<span class='line-break'> </span> Them and Edna are haveing a<span class='line-break'> </span> fine time.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1796">
<h3><a name="page-1796">Thursday, October 21, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>21st  A good day.  Ben finished sowin<span class='line-break'> </span> wheat to day.  Jim went to Long<span class='line-break'> </span> Island this morning for<span class='line-break'> </span> guano and oats.  He got home a<span class='line-break'> </span> bought one o-clock then disked<span class='line-break'> </span> the rest of the day.  Josie is about and<span class='line-break'> </span> that is all.  I got dinner and went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr Owens.  Come home and went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Marvins.  He had bin to Chatham.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie had washed.  I think<span class='line-break'> </span> that they are mad with me.  If<span class='line-break'> </span> I knowed what a bout I would beg forgiveness.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1797">
<h3><a name="page-1797">Friday, October 22, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>22nd  A good day.  Ben &amp; Jim worked<span class='line-break'> </span> on grain land all day.  Ben went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Johnson Reynols and got<span class='line-break'> </span> a little beef.  He went while the<span class='line-break'> </span> horses eat their dinner.  Josie is some<span class='line-break'> </span> better off to day.  To day was my<span class='line-break'> </span> birth day.  I am 74 years old.  Carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> gave me a pair of bedroom slippers and <span class='line-break'> </span> Edna gave me a kiss since [?] she had nothing<span class='line-break'> </span> to give me.  Carrie and the little<span class='line-break'> </span> children come a while this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was so glad they come.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1798">
<h3><a name="page-1798">Saturday, October 23, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>23rd  A good day.  Ben and Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> finished sowing grain to day.  Reese and<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry and I went to Worshams pond.<span class='line-break'> </span> I caught one nice fish.  Dr Owen come<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening and examined Josie and<span class='line-break'> </span> says she must go to a hospidle.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; Josie and the baby went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Jim Powers to night.  They want<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Car to come with them<span class='line-break'> </span> home to help take care of Mabel.<span class='line-break'> </span> I dread the time that we will have.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1799">
<h3><a name="page-1799">Sunday, October 24, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>24th  A good day.  Ben &amp; Josie went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Charlottsvill to day.  Josie went to the hospidle [?].<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Car is here.  Jim staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at home all day.  He has the baby to<span class='line-break'> </span> night trying to get her to sleep.<span class='line-break'> </span> Lee &amp; Grace, Ben East &amp; Elsie and the <span class='line-break'> </span> children and Kate and Pearl and<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie and family all come today.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am a fraid that the baby <span class='line-break'> </span> will cry most of the night.<span class='line-break'> </span> I do hope that Josie may come so she can stay.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1800">
<h3><a name="page-1800">Monday, October 25, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>25th  A good day.  Jim tied tobacco most<span class='line-break'> </span> of the day.  Ben got home tonight from the hospittle.  Josie is very bad<span class='line-break'> </span> off at the hospittle.  Oh I am so sorry <span class='line-break'> </span> for her.  I do hope she may get<span class='line-break'> </span> well.  We are doing the best we<span class='line-break'> </span> can.  The baby cried a lot of<span class='line-break'> </span> of the time last night.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am so troubled I can [not]<span class='line-break'> </span> write as I ought.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1801">
<h3><a name="page-1801">Tuesday, October 26, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>26th  A good day.  Jim and Ben tyed tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> most of the day.  The baby has bin good<span class='line-break'> </span> for her [?].  Carrie come this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning and dressed the baby and Franklin.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ella [?] come this evening.  I dont [know]<span class='line-break'> </span> woh is the most troubled Ella or Carrie.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie come this evening most running.<span class='line-break'> </span> She had heard that Josie had bin opporated<span class='line-break'> </span> on and was doing well.  She was so<span class='line-break'> </span> glad.  I hope she may get well<span class='line-break'> </span> and come home.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1802">
<h3><a name="page-1802">Wednesday, October 27, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>27th  A rainy day most of the time.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim tyed tobacco all day.  Ben went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Charlottsvill to see Josie.<span class='line-break'> </span> I want to hear so bad but I am<span class='line-break'> </span> afraid to hear.  The baby has done as<span class='line-break'> </span> well as we could expect.<span class='line-break'> </span> Betty Hayley washed here today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Did not hang out the clothes.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie come a few minutes this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  We are makeing out<span class='line-break'> </span> as well as I expected.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1803">
<h3><a name="page-1803">Thursday, October 28, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>28th  A good day.  The boys tyed<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco all day.  We have not heard from<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie to day.  Carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> come and dressed the baby.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mollie &amp; Dena come.  I was glad<span class='line-break'> </span> that they come.  I am so sorry<span class='line-break'> </span> that Denia is so mad with<span class='line-break'> </span> all of her folks.  I would do<span class='line-break'> </span> anything in reason to reconcile<span class='line-break'> </span> her but she will not be reasonable.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1804">
<h3><a name="page-1804">Friday, October 29, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>29th  A good day.  Cool.  Some frost this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  Jim moved some tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  Jim hauled<span class='line-break'> </span> some wood.  Ben went to hunt<span class='line-break'> </span> some one to cook.  Did not get any<span class='line-break'> </span> one but got the promice of help.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie come a few minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span> Johnson killed a beef this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  We got some of it.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am so anxious a bout Josie.<span class='line-break'> </span> So a fraid she will never come home.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1805">
<h3><a name="page-1805">Saturday, October 30, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>30  A good day.  A killing frost this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim &amp; Ben tied tobacco all the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Ben went with<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Car home.  Got back at sundown.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie had a card from Josie this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  Carrie washed and dressed<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel &amp; Franklin this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I don't know anything to write<span class='line-break'> </span> to night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1806">
<h3><a name="page-1806">Sunday, October 31, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>31st  A good day.  Jim staid at home.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben went to Charlottsvill.  Has not<span class='line-break'> </span> got back yet.  We all have had<span class='line-break'> </span> a lone some day.  Carrie come a little<span class='line-break'> </span> while this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am a fraid that Josie is <span class='line-break'> </span> bad off so that Ben will not<span class='line-break'> </span> come home to night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1807">
<h3><a name="page-1807">Monday, November  1, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim and Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> tied tobacco all the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Ben carried <span class='line-break'> </span> me &amp; Franklin to White <span class='line-break'> </span> Falls.  I caugh several<span class='line-break'> </span> fish.  I was so glad to<span class='line-break'> </span> go.  Kate come while<span class='line-break'> </span> I was gone.  I was<span class='line-break'> </span> sorry not to see<span class='line-break'> </span> her.  Carrie was here<span class='line-break'> </span> when I come home.<span class='line-break'> </span> She commenced to<span class='line-break'> </span> dress the fish.  Mrs<span class='line-break'> </span> Car helped her.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad for them<span class='line-break'> </span> to helpe me so much.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie come and <span class='line-break'> </span> dressed the baby <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin solde his cow today.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1808">
<h3><a name="page-1808">Tuesday, November  2, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day most of <span class='line-break'> </span> the day.  A little rain<span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  Jim worked on<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco about all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben was one of the <span class='line-break'> </span> judges at the election.<span class='line-break'> </span> I voted to day the first<span class='line-break'> </span> time.  I dont believe<span class='line-break'> </span> it right that woman<span class='line-break'> </span> should vote.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> heard from Josie.  She<span class='line-break'> </span> is getting on as well<span class='line-break'> </span> as could be expected.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Ownen come for<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie and I.  Ben and<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim went to tye<span class='line-break'> </span> tobaco.  Henry went<span class='line-break'> </span> to school.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1809">
<h3><a name="page-1809">Wednesday, November  3, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A beautiful day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Jim &amp; Ben stripped and<span class='line-break'> </span> moved tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  Today was Ednas<span class='line-break'> </span> birth day.  She talked<span class='line-break'> </span> about it a great many<span class='line-break'> </span> times.  Mrs Car gave her<span class='line-break'> </span> some money.  Aunt<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie gave her a nice<span class='line-break'> </span> piece of rbbon and<span class='line-break'> </span> a cake.  I killed<span class='line-break'> </span> a chicken and<span class='line-break'> </span> made pies.  Ben did<span class='line-break'> </span> not hear from Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  He is troubled<span class='line-break'> </span> about not hearing.<span class='line-break'> </span> The baby has bin<span class='line-break'> </span> better to day than usual.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie come this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening and bathed<span class='line-break'> </span> the baby.  I am so<span class='line-break'> </span> glad that she will<span class='line-break'> </span> attend to her.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1810">
<h3><a name="page-1810">Thursday, November  4, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben [&amp;] Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> stripped tobacco most<span class='line-break'> </span> of the day.  Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> killed a hog today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben did not hear from<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie a gain to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie gave me a <span class='line-break'> </span> nice plate of sausage<span class='line-break'> </span> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span> I dont know any<span class='line-break'> </span> thing to write and<span class='line-break'> </span> my pen is so bad<span class='line-break'> </span> that I cant write <span class='line-break'> </span> much.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1811">
<h3><a name="page-1811">Friday, November  5, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The boys<span class='line-break'> </span> stripped tobacco all<span class='line-break'> </span> day and tieing yet<span class='line-break'> </span> 8 tonight.  Ben heard<span class='line-break'> </span> from Josie today.  She<span class='line-break'> </span> is getting on very<span class='line-break'> </span> well.  Carried bathed<span class='line-break'> </span> the baby this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> She brought me some <span class='line-break'> </span> meat and scrapple.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin went to Gretna &amp; Altavista<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  Carrie went <span class='line-break'> </span> to Altavista.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am willing to work all<span class='line-break'> </span> that I am able but <span class='line-break'> </span> the staying so close<span class='line-break'> </span> and studieng how<span class='line-break'> </span> to get every thing<span class='line-break'> </span> done is killing me<span class='line-break'> </span> but I cant help<span class='line-break'> </span> myself.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1812">
<h3><a name="page-1812">Saturday, November  6, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> Jim stripped tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> all day and tonight.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> cooked dinner and<span class='line-break'> </span> put it a way then went<span class='line-break'> </span> fishing.  Reese drove Bens<span class='line-break'> </span> car.  Henry went with<span class='line-break'> </span> us.  I caught one nice<span class='line-break'> </span> fish.  We eat our dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> on the bank of the<span class='line-break'> </span> pond.  Marvin &amp; Carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Strait Stone<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  The [?]<span class='line-break'> </span> come with Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  Ben got<span class='line-break'> </span> a letter from<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> We hope that she<span class='line-break'> </span> is getting on OK.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1813">
<h3><a name="page-1813">Sunday, November  7, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> staid at home<span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  Lizzie came<span class='line-break'> </span> to see us today.  Carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> come and bathe the<span class='line-break'> </span> baby.  She cried<span class='line-break'> </span> all she could.  I am<span class='line-break'> </span> so glad she done it<span class='line-break'> </span> for me as the baby<span class='line-break'> </span> hates bathing so bad.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben went to the<span class='line-break'> </span> hospittle.  Found Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> as well as he could<span class='line-break'> </span> expect.<span class='line-break'> </span> I do hope she may<span class='line-break'> </span> get well soon.<span class='line-break'> </span> Franklin went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Mr Owens<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  We had <span class='line-break'> </span> a big hunt for <span class='line-break'> </span> him.  Carrie made<span class='line-break'> </span> the bread for supper.<span class='line-break'> </span> Lizzie set the table.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1814">
<h3><a name="page-1814">Monday, November  8, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Ben's birth day<span class='line-break'> </span> A good day.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> carried Mrs Car and<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna &amp; Mabel to<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim Powers this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> He eat dinner there.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim &amp; Ben loaded<span class='line-break'> </span> the waggon this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> They intend going to<span class='line-break'> </span> Gretna in the<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  I sowed a<span class='line-break'> </span> little on Effies quilt<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  I am anxious<span class='line-break'> </span> to finish it.<span class='line-break'> </span> A bout all of us<span class='line-break'> </span> have colds.<span class='line-break'> </span> It is lonesome<span class='line-break'> </span> here tonight.  We <span class='line-break'> </span> miss the baby <span class='line-break'> </span> so much.  Hope she<span class='line-break'> </span> wont get sick.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1815">
<h3><a name="page-1815">Tuesday, November  9, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim and Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Gretna with<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco.  John Hutcherson<span class='line-break'> </span> loaded for Owen.<span class='line-break'> </span> Franklin and I staid<span class='line-break'> </span> here most of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span> We went to Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Chatham from<span class='line-break'> </span> Gretna.<span class='line-break'> </span> Heard this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> that Beaula B<span class='line-break'> </span> will be married<span class='line-break'> </span> tomorrow at Lynch<span class='line-break'> </span> Burg.<span class='line-break'> </span> I wish I could <span class='line-break'> </span> know how <span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel is doing<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1816">
<h3><a name="page-1816">Wednesday, November 10, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day and rain<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  Ben went to the<span class='line-break'> </span> mill.  Jim is at Chatham<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Ben went <span class='line-break'> </span> to Jim Powers to see<span class='line-break'> </span> the children tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> There was to be a <span class='line-break'> </span> lecture at the school<span class='line-break'> </span> house.  Henry went.  He<span class='line-break'> </span> has not come home yet.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie and the little<span class='line-break'> </span> children come.  I was <span class='line-break'> </span> glad.  She made bread<span class='line-break'> </span> for our supper.  Guess<span class='line-break'> </span> Bulah was married<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  I sowed some<span class='line-break'> </span> on my quilt.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> heard from Josie.  She<span class='line-break'> </span> is getting on ok I<span class='line-break'> </span> hope.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1817">
<h3><a name="page-1817">Thursday, November 11, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A rainy day.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Gretna for<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim.  Come by Johnson<span class='line-break'> </span> and got some beef.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; Jim and Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> has gone hunting<span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  Franklin<span class='line-break'> </span> and I staid at home<span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  I finished<span class='line-break'> </span> joining a quilt<span class='line-break'> </span> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben heard from <span class='line-break'> </span> Josie to day.  She<span class='line-break'> </span> said that they would<span class='line-break'> </span> let her sit up<span class='line-break'> </span> some today.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1818">
<h3><a name="page-1818">Friday, November 12, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben went<span class='line-break'> </span> to help Oscar a bout<span class='line-break'> </span> his car.  Jim cleaned the<span class='line-break'> </span> hog pen.  They both worked<span class='line-break'> </span> on tobacco some this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim has gone to Marvins <span class='line-break'> </span> to tie tobacco tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben went to Mr Powers<span class='line-break'> </span> to see the children<span class='line-break'> </span> and all the others.  Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> went to school.<span class='line-break'> </span> We had quite a washing<span class='line-break'> </span> here to day.  This morning<span class='line-break'> </span> Hattie Gilbert and I<span class='line-break'> </span> washed until twelve.<span class='line-break'> </span> Then Bettie Haley and<span class='line-break'> </span> Schooler [?] come.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> washed some.  I am<span class='line-break'> </span> glad that it is done.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben heard from Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  She is able to sit<span class='line-break'> </span> up.  I do hope she may<span class='line-break'> </span> soon be so she can<span class='line-break'> </span> come home.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1819">
<h3><a name="page-1819">Saturday, November 13, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A bright colde day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> stripped tobacco.  They eat<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner at Marvins.<span class='line-break'> </span> Franklin staid with Aunt<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie.  Reese and Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> and I went to Worshams<span class='line-break'> </span> Pond.  I wish I had staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at home and worked.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben heard from<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie.  She wants to<span class='line-break'> </span> come home Monday.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Car and the<span class='line-break'> </span> little children<span class='line-break'> </span> are at Jim Powers.<span class='line-break'> </span> I will be glad<span class='line-break'> </span> when they come<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  Earl Booker<span class='line-break'> </span> come with us on<span class='line-break'> </span> the car near Lees<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  She was going <span class='line-break'> </span> to John Emersons<span class='line-break'> </span> to a party tonight.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1820">
<h3><a name="page-1820">Sunday, November 14, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A bright colde day.  Jim staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at home all day.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Mr Powers and<span class='line-break'> </span> brought Mrs Car and <span class='line-break'> </span> the children home<span class='line-break'> </span> then went to Gretna<span class='line-break'> </span> and will go to Charlot<span class='line-break'> </span> and bring Josie home <span class='line-break'> </span> we hope. Kate Harvey come<span class='line-break'> </span> a little while.  Carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> and Marvin went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Jim Thomsons.<span class='line-break'> </span> Joel &amp; [?] Birch<span class='line-break'> </span> was there.  Virginia<span class='line-break'> </span> Wooding stoped here<span class='line-break'> </span> and played with<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna a while this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> The children here<span class='line-break'> </span> has bad coldes.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1821">
<h3><a name="page-1821">Monday, November 15, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A rainy day and<span class='line-break'> </span> colde.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> did not come home.  He<span class='line-break'> </span> phoned he would come<span class='line-break'> </span> tomorrow.  James stripped<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco.  I ironed<span class='line-break'> </span> most of the day.  I<span class='line-break'> </span> churned this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I baked a pumpkin<span class='line-break'> </span> for dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry went to<span class='line-break'> </span> school.<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna &amp; Franklin<span class='line-break'> </span> fussed most of<span class='line-break'> </span> the day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Heard to night<span class='line-break'> </span> that a house<span class='line-break'> </span> burned at<span class='line-break'> </span> Gretna tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am about asleep.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1822">
<h3><a name="page-1822">Tuesday, November 16, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very rainy day<span class='line-break'> </span> one of the worst <span class='line-break'> </span> this year.  Ben has not<span class='line-break'> </span> come home yet.  I am<span class='line-break'> </span> uneasy about them.<span class='line-break'> </span> Hope they will get home<span class='line-break'> </span> ok.  Jim stripped<span class='line-break'> </span> some tobacco.  I have<span class='line-break'> </span> staid in doors as<span class='line-break'> </span> coles [close?] as I could [except?] to<span class='line-break'> </span> milk and bring all<span class='line-break'> </span> the water.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry did not go <span class='line-break'> </span> to school today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna complained<span class='line-break'> </span> of the head ache.  She<span class='line-break'> </span> seems well tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna is very much [?]<span class='line-break'> </span> in what I am writing.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got supper by<span class='line-break'> </span> the fire in the fire<span class='line-break'> </span> place.  Did not make<span class='line-break'> </span> any fire in the range.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1823">
<h3><a name="page-1823">Wednesday, November 17, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A colde windy day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> come home this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie is just from<span class='line-break'> </span> the hospittle.  She looks<span class='line-break'> </span> as well as could be<span class='line-break'> </span> expected.  Jim and<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben stripped some<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco.  Carrie and<span class='line-break'> </span> the little children<span class='line-break'> </span> come a while this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  I think Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> was so glad to see <span class='line-break'> </span> her.  George Emersons<span class='line-break'> </span> barn burned last<span class='line-break'> </span> night with tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> in it.  I am sorry<span class='line-break'> </span> for them.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry did not go<span class='line-break'> </span> to school.  His<span class='line-break'> </span> foot is sore.  He<span class='line-break'> </span> can hardly wear a shoe.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1824">
<h3><a name="page-1824">Thursday, November 18, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim and <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben stripped tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span> John Hutcherson loaded<span class='line-break'> </span> his truck with Maravins<span class='line-break'> </span> and Owens tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span> We all have enjoyed<span class='line-break'> </span> haveing Josie at<span class='line-break'> </span> home today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Hutcherson come<span class='line-break'> </span> to see Josie this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> We was glad to see<span class='line-break'> </span> her.  Mr Jewells<span class='line-break'> </span> house burned up<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  It is a<span class='line-break'> </span> bad thing to have a<span class='line-break'> </span> loss like that.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Car has little <span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel with her tonight<span class='line-break'> </span> up stairs.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1825">
<h3><a name="page-1825">Friday, November 19, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very good day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim and Ben stripped<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco to day.  Bettie Haley<span class='line-break'> </span> washed here to day.  Miss<span class='line-break'> </span> Willie Wooding and Denia<span class='line-break'> </span> Blair and Mollie <span class='line-break'> </span> Reynols come to see<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I stewed and baked<span class='line-break'> </span> pumpkins for dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> I killed two chickens<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening for<span class='line-break'> </span> in the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry went to<span class='line-break'> </span> school.  He is complaining<span class='line-break'> </span> of the tooth ache.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Car and<span class='line-break'> </span> Mabel has gone up stairs.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie come down stairs to dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  We were <span class='line-break'> </span> so glad that<span class='line-break'> </span> she could come.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1826">
<h3><a name="page-1826">Saturday, November 20, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim and <span class='line-break'> </span> Henry stripped tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got breakfast and<span class='line-break'> </span> milked the cows then<span class='line-break'> </span> made and baked bread<span class='line-break'> </span> for dinner and made<span class='line-break'> </span> coffee then dug bait.<span class='line-break'> </span> Reese carried me fishing.<span class='line-break'> </span> We went to White falls.<span class='line-break'> </span> Stopped at Mt Airy.<span class='line-break'> </span> I had a check cashed<span class='line-break'> </span> and bought a bucket<span class='line-break'> </span> of lard.  I come home<span class='line-break'> </span> and churned, salted<span class='line-break'> </span> the butter, then got<span class='line-break'> </span> supper and yet I<span class='line-break'> </span> cant do enough.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben in pertickler<span class='line-break'> </span> dont want to bother<span class='line-break'> </span> with me any wa[y]s.<span class='line-break'> </span> If he thought as much<span class='line-break'> </span> of me as he does of some<span class='line-break'> </span> others I would be glad.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1827">
<h3><a name="page-1827">Sunday, November 21, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim staid at home<span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  I got dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> had chicken and pork.<span class='line-break'> </span> Heard today that Mrs<span class='line-break'> </span> Power has a son born <span class='line-break'> </span> today.  Edna &amp; Franklin<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Marvins today.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to George<span class='line-break'> </span> Blairs.  George &amp; Denia<span class='line-break'> </span> was not at home but<span class='line-break'> </span> come.  They all looked<span class='line-break'> </span> very nice.  Had on new<span class='line-break'> </span> sweaters.  Claud and<span class='line-break'> </span> [?] was there.<span class='line-break'> </span> They were all nice to me<span class='line-break'> </span> and yet I feel that <span class='line-break'> </span> they were not glad <span class='line-break'> </span> to see me.  I went<span class='line-break'> </span> late and had a hard<span class='line-break'> </span> walk.  I got supper<span class='line-break'> </span> after I got home.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1828">
<h3><a name="page-1828">Monday, November 22, 1920</a></h3>

I was<span class='line-break'> </span> very glad to see<span class='line-break'> </span> her.  We did not see<span class='line-break'> </span> any of Marvins folks<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  I ironed some<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  I am so near<span class='line-break'> </span> asleep that I cant<span class='line-break'> </span> write.</p>
</div>

<br />
<div id="page-1829">
<h3><a name="page-1829">Tuesday, November 23, 1920</a></h3>

We<span class='line-break'> </span> are thinkin of going <span class='line-break'> </span> to Danville in the <span class='line-break'> </span> morning if it is not<span class='line-break'> </span> two colde.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have not seen <span class='line-break'> </span> any of Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> people to day. <div id="page-1830">

We had a<span class='line-break'> </span> good time as we<span class='line-break'> </span> could expect.<span class='line-break'> </span> Isila &amp; Cordie Blair<span class='line-break'> </span> come this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad that they<span class='line-break'> </span> come. <div id="page-1831">
<h3><a name="page-1831">Thursday, November 25, 1920</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">

Ben helped<span class='line-break'> </span> Owen kills hogs this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jack Harvey and Mary B<span class='line-break'> </span> come this morning.  They did<span class='line-break'> </span> not say goodby to me<span class='line-break'> </span> but I excuse them.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Wooding and the<span class='line-break'> </span> little children come to<span class='line-break'> </span> see Josie.
